Duan Qirui Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 101

Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan and Seven Others Arrive Together

Warm Welcome from All Sectors, Sun Ke and Others Host Banquet

Duan Talks About Striving for Self-Salvation, Patriotism Has No Division

Temporarily Staying in Shanghai, Will Travel to Hangzhou When the Weather Warms

Duan Qirui, who has been residing in Tianjin, has accepted the invitation of Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, and resolutely traveled south. After arriving in Nanjing, he received a warm welcome from all sides. The night before last, he took the overnight express train from Nanjing to Shanghai and arrived at the North Station at 8:02 a.m. yesterday morning. Over a hundred representatives from various sectors in Shanghai went to the station to welcome him. After disembarking, Duan went to the World Academy Residence on Fooking Road to rest. At noon, Mayor Wu hosted a reception at the Academy. Last night at 7 p.m., Sun Ke hosted a banquet at his private residence on Columbia Road. Various organizations have scheduled a public banquet at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the 27th at noon. When Duan met with reporters from this newspaper yesterday morning, he stated that the only way to save the country is through self-salvation and that patriotism is shared by all, regardless of faction. Details are reported below.

Temporary Security at the North Station Before Duan's arrival, the North Station area was heavily guarded by security teams and police from the Fifth District, with patrols stationed at key points and platforms. The security was particularly tight when Duan's train arrived. Passengers were temporarily prevented from disembarking and all idlers were prohibited from entering the station. Traffic within the platform only returned to normal after Duan and his party left the station.

Warm Welcome from All Sectors Those from the military and political circles in Shanghai who rushed to the North Station yesterday morning to welcome him included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Lin Jin (representative of Garrison Commander Dai Ji), Yang Hu (Director of the Security Department), Wen Hongen (Director of the Public Security Bureau), Chen Jianru (representative of Central Committee member Sun Zhesheng), Chen Boquan (eldest son and representative of Chen Tiaoyuan), Chen Qicai, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Wang Yiting, and others. Representatives from various organizations included Wang Xiaolai and Yu Qiaqing from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Hu Bijiang, Lu Xuepu, and Chen Zheqing from the banking sector, and Duan's old friends Ye Gongchao, Zhang Shizhao, Zheng Hanxiang, Li Sihao, Liang Hongzhi, He Qigong, Chu Huiseng, Fei Baoyan, Tan Daonan, representatives from the Anhui Shanghai Association, Luzhou Association, Satin Trade Association, and Gan Ningqing and citizen representative Zhang Qinghua, who flew to Shanghai from Nanjing, totaling two hundred people. The Municipal Government also sent a military band to play music at the platform to welcome him, creating a very enthusiastic atmosphere.

(Center) Duan Zhirui, Front Row (Left) Duan Honggang (Right) Xu Shiying, Back Row (Left) Wei Zonghan (Right) Wu Guangxin (Photographed by Guowen News Agency)

Duan is Energetic Duan was traveling in a special carriage attached to the Beijing-Shanghai overnight express train. He arrived at the station at exactly 8:02 a.m. Those who came to welcome him boarded the carriage to greet him. Xu Shiying, who accompanied him to Shanghai, introduced them one by one. Duan shook hands and thanked them repeatedly. Then, supported by Wu Guangxin and Xu Shiying, he disembarked and boarded the car that had been prepared on the platform. Amid the lively music of the military band, he drove directly to the World Academy Residence at No. 383 Fooking Road to rest. Hundreds of people stood on both sides of the North Station to admire Duan's demeanor. Duan is now sixty-nine years old and has graying hair, but he is energetic and walks as normally. When he arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning, Duan wore a dark wool hat, an otter collar coat, a blue silk fur robe, and a black satin jacket. Although old, his heroic spirit is still undiminished. Duan lives a simple life, getting up at 6 a.m. every morning to chant scriptures for two hours. He also goes to bed early and chants scriptures for two hours before going to sleep. Those who came to Shanghai with Duan yesterday included Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan, Duan's nephew Honggang, Duan's nephew Chen Xiangfu, Zhong Bojie, and Xu Shiying and Zhang Qun, specially dispatched by the Central Government to accompany him to Shanghai, totaling eight people.

Duan Speaks to Reporters After arriving at the World Academy, Duan went to the guest room on the second floor to rest. He was then introduced by Xu Shiying to meet with reporters from various newspapers. Duan stood up and spoke first, saying that he was old, had been in retirement for many years, had not read newspapers for a long time, and was completely a commoner, not involved in national affairs. This trip south was to visit his younger sister in Nanjing and his second daughter in Shanghai. He was grateful for the warm reception he received from the authorities in Nanjing. As for his opinions on saving the country, he had contributed them to the Central Government to the best of his ability for consideration. He now plans to stay in Shanghai for a while and then travel to Hangzhou when the weather warms up, immersing himself in the famous mountains and appreciating the beauty of the mountains and rivers. When asked about the North China issue by a reporter from this newspaper, Duan replied that the Japanese had reached a point where they were impervious to reason or emotion. The only way for our country to respond is for everyone to be united and work together for self-salvation. As the saying goes, it is better to seek help from oneself than from others. If the whole country is actively prepared and works together, then even ten Japan's would not be fearsome. Our country is facing the consequences of its lack of preparation. Duan concluded with an impassioned speech, saying that patriotism is shared by all and that the only way to save the country is through self-salvation.

Important Figures Visit Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., Duan first met with Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, followed by Dai Ji, Garrison Commander of Songhu, Ye Gongchao, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Shizhao, Yang Shuzhan, Huang Yingbai, and others. Those who visited in the afternoon included Wang Zhengting, Wu Tiyun, Zhang Ji, Fu Zongyao, Deng Hanxiang, Yu Jiegao, Zhang Ming, Wei Zongxin, Li Liejun, Yang Yongtai, Cheng Qian, and others.

Wu and Sun Host Banquets Mayor Wu Tiecheng hosted a banquet at the World Academy yesterday noon to welcome Duan. Important figures from Shanghai were invited to accompany him. At approximately 7 p.m., he attended a banquet hosted by Sun Zhesheng, President of the Legislative Yuan. Many other invitations were declined. In addition, various organizations, such as the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Local Association, the Taxpayers Association, the French Concession Taxpayers Association, the Citizens Federation, the Anti-Civil War League, the Aviation Association, the Northeast Refugee Relief Association, the Volunteer Army Support Association, the Bar Association, the Accountants Association, the General Labor Union, the Education Association, the Zhejiang Provincial Association, and the Exchange Federation, have jointly scheduled a reception at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 12 noon on the 27th. On the same afternoon, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, will host a reception at his residence to welcome Duan.

Duan Has One Son and Four Daughters Duan has one son and four daughters. His son, Hongye, manages the family affairs in Tianjin and will come to Shanghai soon to serve him. His eldest daughter, Shibin, is married to Zhang Daohong, who works at the Salt Affairs Office in Hankou. His second daughter, Wuquan, is married to Fu Lin and currently lives in Shanghai. She is slightly ill. Fu is a student who studied in the United States and once served as Xu Shiying's secretary. His third daughter is married to a nephew of Yuan Shikai and lives in their ancestral home in Henan. His youngest daughter is married to Xi Lun and lives in Qingdao. Duan Honggang, who came with him, is Duan's younger nephew.

First Visit to Shanghai Since the Republic Xu Shiying told reporters yesterday that Duan plans to stay in Shanghai for a while, and his trip to Hangzhou and other places will be postponed until the weather warms up. He recalled that Duan came to Shanghai once after returning to China from Germany in the 29th year of the Guangxu reign. This is the second time, with a gap of more than thirty years. In the sixth year of the Republic, he visited Nanjing once, which was also more than a decade ago.

Wu Guangxin Clarifies Rumors Regarding Duan's visit to the south, it was rumored yesterday that Duan's trip was to suggest direct negotiations between China and Japan to the Central Government. When interviewed by reporters yesterday, Wu Guangxin said that the Japanese rumors are not worth refuting. Duan's character and his history, such as the Constitutional Protection Movement, the campaign against the restoration of the monarchy, and the participation in World War I, prove his integrity. This trip south is to contribute his opinions to the Central Government for their consideration. Duan himself has no preconceived notions.

Aviation to Save the Nation Propaganda Week, Day Two 102

Expressions of Deep Sorrow from All Sectors

Dahua Company Broadcasts Yesterday

The Aviation to Save the Nation Propaganda Week for all sectors in this city was yesterday, the second day. It was originally scheduled for Shi Liangcai and Jiang Huaisu to broadcast speeches. Later, Mr. Shi rescheduled due to personal matters, but Mr. Jiang still arrived at the Dahua Company as scheduled to broadcast. The following is a brief record of his speech:

Jiang Huaisu's Speech

Regarding the significance of the Aviation to Save the Nation Propaganda Week, Mayor Wu has already spoken about it yesterday, and everyone probably already understands. Since the September 18th Incident, "Resist Japan and Save the Nation" can be said to be the unanimous call of the entire populace. However, to see results, there must be a concrete plan. First, we must examine the true facts. Currently, China has a large army, and their morale is also very good, but there has not been substantial progress in national defense. The tools for "Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation" have not been actively replenished. Relying solely on bare hands to fight the enemy will inevitably lead to failure. Among the tools for "Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation," the most important is, of course, airplanes. Mayor Wu said, "In the future, the air force will be the main force in determining victory or defeat." This is very meaningful. During the January 28th Incident last year, although we had the loyal and brave 19th Route Army and the 5th Army, sacrificing blood and flesh to defend our homeland, we suffered significant losses due to the lack of air force support. Just look at the scorched earth of Zhabei and Jiangwan. What should be our feelings? After the January 28th Incident, everyone knew the importance of the air force. Because China's science is backward, we cannot build our own, and the central government's finances are difficult, making it impossible to purchase them, so the strength of the air force simply cannot be strengthened. However, if we have the determination, we should do our best to provide proper assistance to the central government, economic assistance. There are three types of combat aircraft: reconnaissance, bomber, and fighter. Each one costs an average of about 150,000 yuan. This price seems very high, but if we calculate the total losses of the January 28th Incident, it was 150 million yuan, which could have bought 10,000 airplanes. If China had 10,000 airplanes to build its air force and strengthen its national defense, not only would the January 28th Incident in Shanghai not have happened, but perhaps the three northeastern provinces would still be in our hands. France, with the largest air force in the world, has more than 6,000 airplanes. Even small Japan has more than 2,000. Only we in China cannot even give a number, which is very distressing. Now that we have the unanimous determination to "Resist Japan and Save the Nation," we should do our best to help the government build the air force. We must know that "Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation" is not just the government's responsibility, but also the responsibility of our people. "The rise and fall of the nation is the responsibility of every citizen." That is the meaning. Now, Shanghai has the organization of the Aviation Association. The membership fee is two yuan per person, and all the membership fee income will be used to purchase combat airplanes. We hope that the results of this movement, from the "January 28th" airplane to the "Shanghai" airplane, to the "Shanghai Merchant" airplane, to the "Shanghai Worker" airplane, and so on, will continue to rise up. The other day, the Municipal Education Association decided to raise funds to donate the "Shanghai School No. 1" airplane. This small amount is not enough to save the nation. We deeply hope that those with wealth will make large donations. Complete our mission in the near future, otherwise, if the violent Japanese invade Shanghai again, we may not even have the opportunity to pledge donations.

Aviation Association Finds a Location

At 4:00 PM on the 22nd of this month, the Chinese Aviation Association, in order to expand publicity, invited people from all walks of life to the YMCA of the Eight Immortals Bridge, including Central Supervisory Committee member Wu Zhihui and over a hundred others. Chairman Shi Liangcai immediately decided that all attendees would join the association. The Chinese Aviation Association has now found a location at 99 Avenue Joffre to be its headquarters and is actively making arrangements, planning to move in and officially begin operations on February 1st. They will also expand their solicitation of members. The following are the speeches given on that day by Chairman Shi Liangcai, Lin Wojiang, Wu Zhihui, Xue Dubi, Chu Minyi, Mayor Wu, and others:

Shi Liangcai's Speech

Briefly stated, "Our association invited people from all walks of life today to hold this tea party. We are grateful for the gracious attendance of people from all sectors. The significance of our association calling this meeting today is that aviation to save the nation is a matter of utmost urgency today, but how should aviation be planned and developed to achieve the goal of saving the nation? This requires collective wisdom and joint discussion. We earnestly hope that all of you present today will express your opinions to guide us. We still feel indignant when we recall the tragedy of the Japanese airplanes bombing us on January 28th. In the future, we should regard aviation as our second life, quickly catch up, and aim to protect our lives and property so that those bullies have nowhere to use their skills. At the beginning of the establishment of our association, the urgent task is how to raise funds to purchase airplanes. We hope that all sectors will actively assist. It is also very important to consider what use we should make of the airplanes after we purchase them to implement our original intention. Originally, the reason why we spare no effort or expense to seek the development of aviation is to consolidate national defense. There is concern that the airplanes we painstakingly obtain may be used for internal purposes. This is an overthought. In fact, as the national crisis becomes more urgent, anyone with a conscience should work hard to save the nation. There is absolutely no such thing as internal affairs. There is only unity against external enemies, so as not to become sinners of the nation. This is what our association should seriously declare and pay attention to. Now, Mayor Wu has strongly advocated that all staff members of the municipal government, from policemen to security guards, and soldiers, should join our association at the same time. We hope that all of you present today will also join our association, and at any time and place, disseminate information to all sectors to make the people understand the importance of aviation and jointly join our association to work hard. The future of our association really depends on it. Regarding the establishment process of our association, I now invite Mr. Lin Wojiang to report to everyone."

Lin Wojiang's Report

Briefly stated, "Since the 'September 18th' Incident in Shenyang and the 'January 28th' Battle of Songhu, the people of the country have realized the importance of air defense. Party headquarters, local groups, and overseas Chinese have submitted petitions to the National Government, requesting the organization of an Aviation to Save the Nation Association to allow the public to work together to save the nation. The National Government sent this type of report to the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Political Department, which transferred it to the Aviation Administration, summarized the opinions from all parties, and drafted measures. Later, the Aviation Administration sent me, Wojiang, to Shanghai to contact leaders from all sectors. The leaders enthusiastically supported this, and the preparations for the Aviation to Save the Nation Association began. Subsequently, the National Government appointed Mr. Wang Xiaolai and twenty-one others as directors of our association, and Mayor Wu strongly supported us. Our association was officially established on the first of this month. Moreover, because aviation national defense must be sustained for a long time, the name 'Aviation to Save the Nation Association' implies a temporary response, which seems inappropriate. After the government entrusted this idea to Mayor Wu and the preparatory members for consultation, the name was changed to 'Chinese Aviation Association.' This is a general overview of the establishment of our association."

Wu Zhihui's Speech

"Just listening to Mr. Shi Liangcai's speech has moved me very much. Since the Jiawu War, after Japan taught us a lesson, there has been a slogan for saving the nation for almost forty years. Last year, on January 28th, we were taught another lesson. Some people say that if people fight against each other, they must first fight against things before they can fight against people. I used to say that motors save the nation, and aviation uses motors. Now, the purpose of establishing the Chinese Aviation Association is the same as my motor to save the nation doctrine, so I very much agree with it. We must make sure that everyone has motor thinking in their minds in order to like research. There will also be more talents, and science will flourish. Do not say that I am an amateur and ignore it. You must know that everything always starts with amateurs becoming professionals. When everyone becomes a professional, then you can fight against others. You must not embrace non-resistance and then have others teach you a lesson. It is too late. If the 400 million people in our country talk about raising funds, it is really like a drop in the bucket, but some people say that the people are extremely poor and cannot afford it. You should know that even if the cow is thin, this hair is easy to pull out, so I advise the people of the country to first change this way of thinking, hurry up and cultivate talents, and everyone use the motor to save the nation doctrine. This is developing aviation to save the nation."

Xue Dubi's Speech

Briefly stated, "Your association is named the Aviation Association. I would just like to speak on the word 'Association.' There is a Chinese proverb that says, 'One tree cannot support a tall building.' Another proverb says, 'United will is an impregnable stronghold.' The former means that holding on alone weakens the momentum, while the latter means that the crowd makes things easy to lift. For decades, our country has been invaded because tens of thousands of people and tens of thousands of minds could not unite and cooperate. Now, seeing the establishment of your association, it is due to the joint efforts of the government and public organizations. This is enough to prove that the government and the public have the greatest awareness and thoroughly understand the need to work together to resist the enemy. From now on, I hope that this one word of sincerity will break the current crisis facing our country."

Chu Minyi's Speech

"Just now, Mr. Wu Zhihui spoke about the method of the Chinese Aviation Association raising funds, which is very easy, but there must be a centralized method, or each group donates one airplane, or each individual donates one airplane. The whole country should quickly establish branches and proceed in a unified manner, with each person soliciting individually. The more the better, naturally we will be able to achieve the degree that we hope for, and aviation to save the nation can be put into practice."

Wu Tiecheng's Speech

"Just now, Mr. Wu Zhihui said that 'After our country suffered a heavy blow from Japan in the Jiawu War, the people of the country issued a slogan for saving the nation, but almost forty years have passed, and the country has still not been saved, and is even more dangerous. The unexpected arrival of the September 18th Incident the year before last was so overwhelming that there was no way to resist it, which is very painful. We must know that saving the nation must focus on reality, and it is definitely not as effective as the empty words of the past. If we continue in this way, then even if Mr. Wu reaches the age of seventy or eighty, he will still be listening to a lifetime of chaotic talk about saving the nation. What benefit will it have to the actual saving of the nation? The actual work of saving the nation today is to build national defense. Regardless of all sectors of the public, whether they are scholars, farmers, workers, or merchants, they should all make a painful decision and take the construction of national defense as the central undertaking. If they can work hard, then after five or ten years, there will be considerable results to see. Otherwise, if you take individual concepts as the center, there will be no effect. What benefit will it have to the country? The deep wounds and deep pain of the January 28th Incident in Shanghai last year were really beyond the imagination of anyone beforehand. From this, we can see how important air defense is. At present, the power of the air force is greatest in France. The French have said arrogantly that they can destroy the entire city of London in a few minutes. In the past, there were tanks to deal with the army, and submarines to deal with the navy. Now, weapons of murder are becoming more and more powerful. After having air force bombing, it is necessary to have air defense equipment. After we have received the serious lessons of the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, we should thoroughly awaken and take the construction of national defense as the center of all undertakings. However, this matter is important and must be done by the people of the whole country, working together with one heart, in order to succeed. My brother has seen this, so I have advised all staff members of the government, as well as security guards and police officers, etc., numbering in the thousands, to join the Aviation Association as an example. Shanghai has about 3 million people in the entire city. Even if each person pays an ordinary membership fee of two yuan per year, there will be an annual income of 6 million yuan, which can purchase or manufacture dozens of airplanes. The national defense of Russia, France, and Japan all relies on the automatic construction of the people. If our country wants to resist Japan and save the country, why is it any different? Therefore, I hope that all the citizens of Shanghai will join the Aviation Association, and that the entire province and the entire country will be like this. Then our national defense will have a solution, and we will not have to worry about not having a day to seek revenge and avenge our humiliation."

The City Chamber of Commerce Leads the Propaganda 103

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce leads the city's business community to carry out aviation to save the nation propaganda. A Letter to Merchants 104

Yesterday, the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce issued a letter to merchants throughout the city, saying, "The Songhu Anti-Japanese War lasted thirty-four days. The officers and soldiers were loyal to the country, and the citizens provided support for the army. It was not that we did not work together with all our strength to defend Shanghai, but why were the factories reduced to ashes and the city transformed into ruins? More than hundreds of thousands of residents throughout the city suffered losses, all because of the bombings by a few airplanes and the fact that our air defense equipment was non-existent, allowing them to enter unchallenged. When the incident first occurred, merchants generally discussed taking out war insurance to compensate for the losses, but insurance companies consulted their headquarters, worried that the risk was too great, and all refused to underwrite. Therefore, very few people had war insurance during this battle, and the unexpected losses were irreparable. This is probably the most unforgettable thing for our merchants. As the saying goes, 'It is better to ask oneself than to ask others.' It is better to prepare for a rainy day than to dig a well when thirsty. Today, if a country wants to stand in the world, a prosperous city must first have air defense equipment to deal with emergencies. Moreover, the situation in our country is like a bird's nest on a dangerous curtain, constantly facing the possibility of being attacked. We should not be slack and unprepared. Now, the price of combat airplanes is about 100,000 yuan each. Public funds are tight, and although there are annual purchases, it is not easy to become a spectacle. If the merchants do not raise funds and donate them, then our country's fledgling air force will remain immature forever. If something happens one day, how can we defeat the enemy? During the Songhu battle, the Japanese airplanes gathered at the front line, including both naval and military aircraft, totaled only one hundred or so, according to the newspapers at the time. If our merchants can raise 20 million yuan, we can purchase 200 airplanes. Although we dare not say that we can dominate the airspace, we can consolidate Shanghai's defenses. This 20 million yuan is only one-tenth of the losses from the Shanghai war. The international situation is becoming increasingly dangerous, and future wars, relying on the renewal of their weapons, will only tend towards expansion. If we continue to delay, then the losses in the future may be ten or a hundred times more than after the Songhu battle. Once this opportunity is lost, it will be too late to regret it. Therefore, to put it bluntly, the people's cry for aviation to save the nation can be said to be the only way for merchants to save themselves, and its effect is a million times better than war insurance. Only when our merchants rise up together can we achieve it."

Miao Zhongxiu Discusses China's Silk Industry 116

Since being affected by the global economic downturn, China's silk industry has gradually declined, leading to the closure of silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and the unemployment of workers, accumulating to tens of thousands. The impact not only affects the silk industry itself but is also the most pressing economic problem for our country today. Yesterday, a reporter specifically visited Mr. Zhongxiu, the Director of the Raw Silk Inspection Department of the Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry. According to him, last year's exports of Shanghai raw silk totaled 40,513 bales (including 17,847 bales of Jiangsu-Zhejiang factory silk), a decrease of 21,430 bales compared to 1931, a decrease of 34,542 bales compared to 1930, and an even greater decrease of 74,217 bales compared to 1929. Guangzhou's exports last year totaled approximately 31,870 bales (estimated 2,000 bales in December), a decrease of 14,700 bales compared to 1931 and a decrease of 28,600 bales compared to 1920. Compared to 1929, the decrease was 32,360 bales. The disastrous decline in China's raw silk foreign trade is as described above. However, Japan's raw silk exports last year totaled approximately 545,521 bales (estimated 50,000 bales in December), a decrease of only 8,077 bales compared to 1931, but an increase of 71,641 bales compared to 1930. In terms of US consumption, last year's usage of Japanese silk was 518,794 bales, not only not decreasing compared to 1911 but actually increasing by 13,014 bales. Consumption of Chinese silk was only 22,047 bales, a decrease of 44,118 bales compared to 1931. From this, it can be seen that China's silk industry, after being hit by the global economic downturn, has continued to decline, while Japan, since 1920, has been making vigorous progress and has restored its inherent prosperity. This is based on the cooperation of all levels of society in Japan, but also due to the preparations of the silk industry itself. What is this preparation? It is the scientific and rationalization of the entire silk industry. This preparation cannot be achieved in a day or two, nor can it be created by the efforts of one party. It is the result of decades of cooperation between the government, merchants, and experts. The biggest shortcoming of China's silk industry is that there is too little silk of the same grade. Jiangsu-Zhejiang factory silk has some that are above 90 points and some that are below 70 points. The production is small, and the grades are complicated. What the United States needs is a large quantity of raw silk of the same grade, which is the opposite of the production situation of Chinese raw silk. It is enough to see that the sales of Chinese silk in the United States are decreasing daily. It is hoped that the government will actively promote it, merchants will work hard, and use the wisdom of experts. With the joint cooperation of these three forces, China's silk industry may have hope.

Yu Qiaqing's Mediation of the Wusong Ship Case Yields No Results 121

The Company's Attitude is Strong, Yu is Hesitant to Go Again

The Coordination Association Shelves the Matter Temporarily Due to Difficult Cooperation Between the Two Parties

Regarding the case of the Wusong Ship expelling workers, Chinese Director Yu Qiaqing negotiated with the company's manager yesterday, but there were no results due to the company's firm attitude. Whether the Coordination Association will be established is still undecided. Details are recorded as follows:

Support Meeting. The support meeting for the Wusong Ship tragedy was held at 2:15 PM yesterday at the Zhongcang Guild Hall at No. 36 Jiuxiaochang Road. Thirty-nine representatives from various ships attended. Chuan Xiaoting chaired the meeting, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) It is proposed to request the Party and government authorities to continue mediation. (2) If this case is not resolved in the near future, it is decided to send personnel to Beijing to petition the Central Party Headquarters. (3) For the two sailors, Ma Qiaogen and Wu Ruiqing, who were arrested and escorted to Shanghai, apart from Ma, who has been released, the authorities will try to rescue Wu and release him.

Uncertain Resumption of Work. Wei Biansheng, a clerk recruited by the donation department of the Wusong Ship Tragedy Support Association, told a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday that it is currently difficult to predict whether this case can be resolved immediately. The anger of the workers is inevitable. However, with the supervision of the various committee members, no out-of-bounds actions will occur. All ships have given their sympathetic assistance, which is very appreciated. The company's firm attitude, it is thought that justice will never be bent to its will. As for whether Chinese Director Yu Qiaqing will go to negotiate today (i.e., yesterday), no notice has been received from Mr. Yu. There are outside rumors that Zhang Xianming, the newly appointed compradore of the Wusong Ship, sent personnel to negotiate the resumption of work and that there will be a full resumption of work after three shifts, but these are not true.

Association Not Established. Initially, it was proposed that the Mutual Aid Association and the Zhongcang workers jointly form a Coordination Association. The Mutual Aid Association had requested the prior release of the compradore Jing Chunhua and accountant Hu Henian, who were arrested in Hankou, as a condition for cooperation. After investigation, it was found that Hu and the others were still bailed out by the Mutual Aid Association themselves. The Party and government authorities were concerned that the Mutual Aid Association would not be able to cooperate, so they started discussions at the Seafarers' Special Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM yesterday. Wang Xianqing, Director of the Mediation Section of the Bureau of Social Affairs, Zhou Lianze, Chief Executive of the People's Training Section representing the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yu Jiayong, Standing Member of the Seafarers' Party Headquarters, and Secretary Xu Shiqi attended. According to Xu Shiqi's remarks to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency, whether the Coordination Association is established depends on whether the labor and management can cooperate. If the association is established but the opinions are different, then the establishment of this association is worthless. Therefore, it is difficult to announce whether it will be established now. In short, the Party and government authorities are still entrusting the Mutual Aid Association to be responsible for mediation.

Mediation Hopeless. According to Chinese Director Yu Qiaqing, the labor and management in the Wusong Ship case entrusted mediation last time. The meeting was not held because the Taikoo manager was away from home the day before yesterday. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Mr. Yu went to meet with the manager, Hote (transliteration). After a long conversation, the manager's attitude was very firm, and there was no room for mediation. The manager also said that the dismissal of the tea servers was for the convenience of the passengers. The Wusong Ship now only employs more than 30 Western waiters. In the future, the name "tea server" may be abolished. Among the tea servers on each ship, some are good, but many are bad, etc. It is heard that Mr. Yu said that the company's attitude is so strong that the future is hopeless, so he expressed that he has no intention of serving as a mediator again.

Decision to Wait. The laid-off employees held a general meeting at the Jinli Wharf Labor Union at 2:00 PM yesterday. Verdi, Director General of the French Municipal Council, Issues a Statement Regarding the Cross-Border Road and Telephone Case 123

According to the Continental News, Verdi, Director General of the French Municipal Council, stated the truth to a reporter from this newspaper yesterday (23rd) because of a report that Chen, the Chief of the Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau, said that the cross-border road construction and telephone case was delayed due to the sudden objection from the French Concession authorities. Verdi said that the French Concession Public Works Bureau had long agreed to the terms of the contract completely, but disagreed with the implementation method set by the Public Concession Municipal Council. Although the contract has not been signed, the representatives of the Shanghai Telephone Company, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, and the two Concession authorities have all agreed. At this time, the unresolved dispute lies only in the implementation aspect. The contract stipulates that the Shanghai Telephone Bureau will be reimbursed 60 yuan per telephone installed along the roads built across the border in the northern district each year and 12 yuan per telephone installed along the roads built across the border in the western district each year. The Municipal Council proposed that this increased cost be borne by all users, while the French Municipal Council thought that this was one of the inconveniences for those living outside the Concession and should not be borne by users living within the Concession. However, this method of bearing the cost is not stipulated in the contract, so this matter is only a point of contention between the two Concession authorities and is unrelated to the contract itself. Now, the Municipal Council proposes that all users bear this cost for only one year. If there are similar burdens in the future, they will be borne by users living outside the Concession. After the telephone company solves this case, the increased income may make it possible for the company to appropriately reduce telephone charges after one year. Therefore, the French Concession authorities are not very persistent now and may agree to this temporary measure. This matter will be submitted for discussion at the regular meeting of the Board of Directors of the French Municipal Council next Monday. If it is agreed, the cross-border road construction telephone contract can be signed on a scheduled date.

Bravery of Police Officers in Capturing Thieves in an Armed Robbery on Shiqing Road, All Culprits Apprehended 129

Thieves Refuse Arrest from Upstairs, Both Sides Exchange Fire Over 20 Rounds

One Thief Accidentally Shot and Killed by an Accomplice, Succumbs to Severe Wounds

Yesterday morning, a robbery occurred at the residence of Mr. Pan, a native of Huzhou, located at No. 1, Lane 285, Shiqing Road, Zhabei. Pan's eldest daughter seized an opportunity to rush to the local police station to report the incident and request immediate arrest. Patrol Officer Gao Ziqiang led several armed officers to the scene and successfully apprehended three thieves, while one thief died. The details are as follows:

Background of the Victim: Mr. Pan, a resident of No. 1, Lane 285, Shiqing Road, Zhabei, resides in a new three-story building. Pan is over sixty years old and has been employed as a credit officer at a silk shop for more than ten years. Diligent and thrifty, he is highly trusted by the shop owner. Pan has two sons and three daughters. His eldest son is married and also works at the silk shop, while his second son works at a silk shop in Xiaodongmen. The family lives harmoniously.

Four Thieves Rob: At 9:30 a.m. yesterday, four robbers dressed in luxurious silk robes suddenly knocked on the side door of Pan's residence. The maid, unaware of their intentions, opened the door and let them in. The robbers falsely claimed to be from the defense corps searching for opium. Two of the robbers brandished pistols to intimidate, while the other two went upstairs to rob. Pan's eldest daughter, Qingfen, seized the opportunity to rush to the Shiqing Road police station to report the incident and request immediate arrest. Patrol Officer Gao Ziqiang, upon receiving the report, immediately led officers Wang Zhejing and Zhao Jinzhong to the scene. They bravely stormed into Pan's residence and forcefully subdued two robbers downstairs, disarming them.

Accidental Killing: As the two robbers were struggling, the two robbers upstairs heard the commotion and, realizing the situation was unfavorable, hid at the top of the stairs and opened fire to resist arrest, putting up a strong defense. Both sides exchanged fire, creating a scene reminiscent of a major battle, with more than twenty rounds fired. As a result, the robbers upstairs accidentally shot one of their accomplices in the head. The bullet entered the left side of his face and exited the back of his head, causing him to fall to the ground immediately, his brains splattered.

Recovered Loot: At that time, more than ten patrol officers from the Fifth District Headquarters, hearing the alarm, rushed to surround the area. Soon, one robber jumped down from the back room and was captured. The police found $100 yuan on his person, and under the bed in the living room, they found

All Culprits Apprehended: One robber was hiding under the bed upstairs. The officers pulled him out by his legs and apprehended him, seizing a pistol and six bullets. In total, the four wounded robbers were taken to the district headquarters. According to their confessions, one robber was named Li Changting, 26 years old, from Haimen, residing at Room 317, Da Zhonghua Hotel, Xizang Road; one robber was named Wang Zailin, 22 years old, from Chongming; and one robber was named Huang Ziwen, 24 years old, from Wuxi, residing at No. 19, Gongping Inn. The wounded robber was unable to speak. According to the three robbers, his name was Xu Afu, from Haimen. District Chief Jin Gong hired workers to take the wounded robber to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but he succumbed to his injuries due to excessive blood loss at around 2:00 p.m. yesterday. The remaining three robbers were sent to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for legal processing.

Committed Suicide by Poison After Business Closed

Robbery at Xiangfen Lane Solved in One Hour 132

Commendable Diligence of the Police Detectives

Thieves Should Know to Exercise Restraint

Since the beginning of winter, robberies have been rampant, occurring several times a day. In view of this, Public Concession Police Criminal Division Chief Detectives Lu Liankui and You A'gen issued special instructions to all Chinese detectives in each police station to patrol their respective jurisdictions in groups, day and night, to prevent crime. At 11:30 a.m. the day before yesterday, the Huasheng Electric Appliance Store at No. 484, Yixin Lane, Xiangfen Lane, Nanjing Road, was suddenly invaded by five robbers. After searching and looting for a long time, they obtained $450 yuan and fled in different directions. Among the robbers, Wen Bingrong, a native of Wuxi, and Li Wenming, a native of Hebei, were seen by Huang Fusen, a Chinese detective from the General Patrol Department, while patrolling the street. Suspecting their behavior, he followed them. Seeing them enter the Da Zhonghua Hotel on Xizang Road, he was about to apprehend them when the two men came out again. Huang continued to follow them to the Jiangsu Automobile Company on Guizhou Road. The two robbers were about to call a car to Hongkou. Seeing that the situation was urgent, Huang immediately called Zhao Ziren, a Chinese detective chief, and Bao Yutang, a policeman, from the Lao Zha Police Station to assist in arresting Wen and Li. They were taken back to the police station. After questioning, Yao Gengsheng, a native of Shanghai, was arrested in Room 526 of the Da Zhonghua Hotel, and Li Yunxuan, a native of Wuxi, Weng Linsheng, a native of Shanghai, Zeng Xiangsheng, a native of Shanghai, Ping Genlin, a native of Suzhou, Shen Hesheng, a native of Huzhou, and Li A'da, a native of Chongming, were successively arrested in Room 3, Anle Hotel, Baoyu Lane, Edward Road. A pistol, 194 bullets, and stolen money of $136.5 yuan were seized and taken to the police station. In total, the case was solved in just one hour from the time it occurred to the time of arrest, which is extremely fast. Yesterday morning, the case was transferred to the First Special Court's Criminal Division One. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, prosecuted Wen Bingrong, Li Wenming, Yao Gengsheng, and Li Yunxuan under Article 348 of the Criminal Law. The other defendants were detained for further investigation. Zeng Xiangsheng hired Fan Gang as his lawyer. Presiding Judge Qian Hongye briefly questioned the defendants and ordered them to be remanded in custody for further questioning at a later date.

During the Day a Maid, at Night Accompanied the Master in Bed 133

Cao Jiaorong Accuses Master of Rape Resulting in Pregnancy

Judge Suggests Best to Settle Out of Court

Tao Dahai, a professional foreign goods broker, rented a house with his concubine Tao Wangshi (named Wang Laosan) at No. 1, Liangshan Lane, Pingji Road, last autumn. They schemed to drug Cao Jiaorong, a 21-year-old maid from Ningbo, with wine, and then raped her. Unexpectedly, this one encounter resulted in a secret pregnancy. As the maid was a widow, it was difficult for her to face her in-laws with a pregnancy. Therefore, she hired lawyer Wu Peng to file a rape lawsuit in the First Special District District Court against Tao Dahai, Wang Laosan, and the introducer Lu A'xiang (also known as He Xiang). The lawsuit also included a civil suit, requesting the court to order the defendants to pay alimony of $25 yuan per month. The lawsuit stated that the plaintiff, due to the death of her husband, had only one remaining aunt-in-law and two young children to support. Forced by livelihood, she left her aunt-in-law and children to seek a living in Shanghai. On July 24, she was introduced by her fellow villager Lu A'xiang to work as a maid at Tao's house for a monthly salary of $6 yuan. Later, because the Tao family had another girl who also needed care, the salary was increased by $4 yuan. On the second day of her service, Tao and Wang paid her $20 yuan in advance, saying that they were issuing it in advance because of her poor family circumstances. The plaintiff was grateful for the consideration of the male and female masters and did not know that they had other intentions. Unexpectedly, on the evening of August 1, Tao and Wang colluded to set up a situation, preparing wine and dishes, and treating her with good intentions, even drugging the plaintiff and making her unable to resist. They committed rape. After sobering up, she was filled with sorrow and despair. Tao consoled her in bed, and Wang Laosan also used inducements and threats, saying that because she had no children, if she conceived, she would be heavily rewarded and made the main wife. She was subsequently raped several times. Unexpectedly, after Tao's lust was satisfied, he became tired of her. Although she was already pregnant, he broke his promise and, together with Wang Laosan, began to abuse her. Wang had an opium addiction and needed $5 yuan a day to satisfy it. She repeatedly used a opium needle to stab the plaintiff all over her body. On October 28, she was forced to leave and could not return to her hometown. The defendants' actions were obviously illegal. Therefore, she filed a lawsuit in accordance with Articles 240 and 244 of the Criminal Law and Article 337, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, requesting that they be punished as they deserve and also filing a civil lawsuit to deter illegal acts and protect women's rights. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qian Wenji opened the trial. Only Wang Laosan was absent due to illness. Tao and Lu both surrendered to the court with lawyers Fan Gang for questioning. According to Cao Jiaorong, after she became pregnant after being raped, Tao Dahai was extremely happy. In addition to making silk clothes for her, he ordered his concubine Wang Laosan to accompany her to Dr. Chen Xiaobao's clinic at Yimiao for diagnosis and to take miscarriage prevention medication. However, Tao Dahai completely denied the allegations. Lu A'xiang only admitted to introducing the plaintiff to work at Tao's house and did not know about the other matters. Later, Xia, a neighbor of Tao, testified that another maid who had been dismissed by Tao's family said that Cao Jiaorong was a servant during the day and a wife at night. This was hearsay, and whether it was true was not known. Judge Qian believed that it was best to settle this type of case privately, so he ordered the case to be rescheduled and instructed both parties to mediate outside the court.

County-Designated Beiqiao Work and Rest Bell 135

Ancient Bell of Mingxin Temple is One of the Few Antiquities

Invigorate National Spirit and Reform Laziness

The Shanghai County Bureau of Education suggested to the County Government yesterday that the ancient bell of Mingxin Temple in Beiqiao be designated as a work and rest bell. The document stated that the chief of the Zhuanqiao Farmer Education Center, Zhang Yi, reported that the ancient bell of Mingxin Temple in Beiqiao is one of the few antiquities in our county. The county chief and people from all walks of life initiated and sponsored the collection of funds to repair the bell. The preservation of antiquities will rival Tang sculptures. At a time when foreign disasters are imminent and customs are lazy and extravagant, awakening the vigilance of the people and invigorating the national spirit is an urgent task for today. This year's center has a plan to set up an alarm bell. Recently, reading a newspaper report that the Department of Education ordered each county to set up a work and rest bell to invigorate the national spirit and reform folk laziness, I feel the necessity of setting up the bell even more. The ancient bell of Mingxin Temple in Beiqiao is large in shape and loud in sound, making it most suitable for use as a work and rest bell. In addition to preparing funds to equip the center with its own work and rest bell to supplement the inadequacy of the ancient bell of Mingxin Temple, I respectfully submit this document to the director of the bureau, suggesting that the County Government designate the ancient bell of Mingxin Temple in Beiqiao as a work and rest bell to warn and save the nation. This is in the public interest.

Regulations for Western Doctors Before 1929 to Apply for a Practicing Certificate 137

The Municipal Health Bureau previously drafted regulations for Western doctors who registered and obtained licenses in Shanghai before 1929 to apply for a practicing certificate. The original text is as follows: "Regulations for Western Doctors Who Registered and Obtained Licenses in Shanghai Before 1929 to Apply for a Practicing Certificate" (1) Any Western doctor who has the qualifications specified in Article 2, Paragraph 1 of the Ministry of Interior's Provisional Certificate Issuance Method for Doctors (i.e., has been practicing in a well-equipped hospital for more than five years) and has practiced in this city before 1929 may apply to the Health Bureau for a practicing certificate. The Minghan couple were old, frail, and often ill, and burdened with family affairs, so they did not notice Ms. Xue's ill intentions. In the autumn of that year, Shuangqin accompanied her mother to Wing On Company for shopping, and they met the defendant on the way. They also went to Wing On Company, and the defendant bought a delicate watch and a bottle of perfume, along with the invoice, and placed them in front of Shuangqin before leaving. Afterwards, the defendant took advantage of Shuangqin's acquaintance with Ms. Hanyun to entice Shuangqin to go to cafes for snacks. A few days later, he lured her to watch a movie. One day, he invited Shuangqin to take a drive in his car, and at mealtime, they

went to the Cangzhou Hotel. Shuangqin, young and ignorant, thought the hotel was just a place to eat, but unexpectedly, she was led into a room and subjected to all sorts of enticements and deceits. Shuangqin sternly refused and tried to escape, but the door was locked, and the defendant claimed that he was currently in a divorce lawsuit with his wife, and as soon as the lawsuit was over, he would marry Shuangqin. Shuangqin, through his deception and coercion, was forced to lose her virginity. To this day, she thinks of it with deep hatred. Afterwards, he occasionally invited her out, sometimes to eat, sometimes to watch movies, or to go to hotels. This went on for over a year. In the winter of 1928, the defendant was accused of a criminal offense and fled. In May 1930, he saw Shuangqin again and employed the same old tricks,

renting the house at No. 32, LaFayette Road, LaFayette Lane, for Shuangqin to live in. He himself would come occasionally in his free time. Later, the defendant began to go out and return with his wife's niece, their relationship unclear, and people gossiped. He became increasingly cold towards Shuangqin. In July of this year, the defendant's rented house at No. 130, Guofu Road, was due to expire, and Shuangqin moved in. The defendant went from being cold to completely abandoning her. When Shuangqin personally went to his house to inquire, he initially evaded her, but later ignored her. When she sent letters to question him, he also did not reply. Shuangqin hired a lawyer to send a letter of inquiry, and the defendant commissioned his friend Niu Menmian to entrust Ms. Yu Suqi to mediate with Shuangqin, willing to give 3,000 yuan to terminate the relationship. Shuangqin replied that being seduced and losing her virginity could not be settled with money alone. She only thinks that

Shuangqin, a girl from a good family, had always received a good upbringing. Unfortunately, her family was neighbors with the defendant, and she was deceived by him, seduced and abandoned. The facts are clear, and Shuangqin hates him to the core and has no way to seek justice. The defendant has committed the crime of seduction under Article 257, Paragraph 1, and the crime of abandonment under Article 310, Paragraph 1, of the Criminal Law, and requests that he be punished according to the law. Subsequently, the court summoned the defendant, and the defendant hired lawyer Qiu Fenling to present a defense, stating that the elements of seduction or abduction under Article 257 of the Criminal Law require that the seduction be of a man or woman under the age of twenty, separating them from their parent or guardian who has parental rights. According to the plaintiff Yan Shuangqin, she is now twenty-five years old. According to the plaintiff's statement, she only began to

cohabit in LaFayette Lane in 1930. Shuangqin was already twenty years old at that time, and the provisions of the aforementioned article cannot be applied. There is already Interpretation Example No. 224 of the Seventeenth Year to interpret this. As for this case, it was Shuangqin who seduced the defendant, not the defendant who abducted Shuangqin. At that time, Shuangqin and the defendant lived in the same neighborhood. One was a girl from a small family, naturally romantic, and the other was the son of a prominent family, a scholar by nature. Shuangqin admired the defendant for being handsome and wealthy. Initially, her eyes followed him, moving her spirit, and she began to seduce him. Later, she wrote letters in her own hand, asking to meet him in a certain place. The sentiments were tangled and impossible to finish reading.

The defendant was at the prime of his youth and was eventually overturned. The letters are still there; how can she deny it? (There are as many as eleven letters.) Moreover, the house on LaFayette Road was rented by Shuangqin through her brother-in-law, Zheng Shifan (who has already been sentenced to life imprisonment for kidnapping Pu Wenting and others). Therefore, the defendant did not initially know the details of the house address, as evidenced by Shuangqin's letters. The so-called separation from those who have parental rights is even more untenable. Now that Shuangqin has never acquired the status of a family member of the defendant,

the defendant has no obligation to support her. However, the defendant is benevolent and has given her money from time to time. How can there be any abandonment to speak of? Moreover, Shuangqin is only twenty-five years old, neither old nor young, and has no disabilities. The responsibility of abandonment under criminal law is even more difficult to establish. In short, the plaintiffs are fabricating accusations and have ulterior motives. This case was heard yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM by Judge Wang Gangxu in the Criminal Court No. 1. He first questioned the plaintiffs and then the defendant, who stated that he was 36 years old and that he met the plaintiff in 1930, not six years ago. The rented house was rented by Shuangqin herself through her brother-in-law. In July of this year, Shuangqin moved into Guofu Road without the defendant's consent. However, the defendant's feelings for Shuangqin

were not lost. It was because her relatives were involved in a kidnapping case, and the defendant advised her to break away from them, but she refused, hence the estrangement. However, the defendant still gave her over a thousand yuan for expenses in February and did not neglect to support her. The plaintiff's lawyer claimed that the defendant had been committing adultery with Shuangqin for six years. There is now written evidence from the defendant himself, and his friends Niu Men and Ms. Yu Suqi can testify. The witness Ms. Yu Suqi then testified in court, proving that the defendant had entrusted Niu Men to explain to her that the two had known each other for six years. Yan Shuangqin claimed that the house in LaFayette Lane was rented by her with 1,000 yuan given to her by the defendant. The questioning continued until 6:30 PM. Judge Wang ordered the defendant to provide bail and be available at any time and directed both parties to try to reconcile privately, adjourning the hearing to another day.

If one type of the above items is insufficient to prove, several additional proof documents may be ordered to be supplemented. B. A curriculum vitae. C. Two 2-inch half-length photos. Precautions for the Lunar New Year's Eve 141

Public Security Bureau:

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, under Director Wen, recently stated that defense is important during the winter defense period, and there will inevitably be more violations of police regulations during the Lunar New Year. Yesterday, he specifically instructed all section and department staff to arrive at the bureau on time every day. Even on Lunar New Year's Day, they must be at their desks to handle official business to avoid delaying important matters. He also ordered the section and team leaders in each district to increase patrols day and night during Lunar New Year's Eve and New Year's Day to strengthen defenses.

Police Station:

Today is Lunar New Year's Eve. Although the business community has implemented the Gregorian calendar, many still use the old lunar calendar. It is customary to close accounts and collect debts everywhere. The Shanghai Municipal Police, deeply concerned that thieves and bandits will take the opportunity to be active, has strictly ordered all police stations under its jurisdiction that all Chinese and Western police officers on duty are not allowed to leave the police station and must be on standby. All Chinese and Western detectives will be fully armed and patrolling everywhere, and a car patrol team will be formed to drive motorcycles and inspect the roads. The Gordon Road reserve team will also be fully deployed. In addition to the original posts, double posts will be added to each road, and plainclothes detectives will be stationed in each secluded place. Armored vehicles equipped with machine guns will continuously patrol key areas to prevent petty criminals from being active.

The Shanghai International Combined Racing is scheduled to start at 1:30 PM on the 26th of this month. It is heard that there will be a total of seven races on that day, and the charity special prize race will be the fifth race. The race club will begin drawing the numbers at 2:00 PM, distributing them to the horses starting in the fifth race. After the race, the numbers of the first three horses will be the winning numbers.

Police Station Suspends Handling Criminal Cases for Four Days 143

The Shanghai First Special District Court and the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court will continue to operate as usual during the Lunar New Year. However, the Shanghai Municipal Police will follow the old practice and close for three days from January 26 (i.e., Lunar New Year's Day) to January 28. Since January 29 is also a regular Sunday holiday, the police stations will suspend handling criminal cases for four days. During this period, the First Special Court will only hear privately prosecuted criminal cases, which will continue as usual. In addition, civil lawsuits will still be heard daily.

Fundraising Under the Pretense of Relief for Volunteer Army, Squandering Funds on Prostitutes 144

| Is It Right To Eat Zhao Yanru Et Al's Flesh? |

Zhao Yanru, a native of Anhui who previously worked in a certain army, was dismissed from his post for some reason. Idling and addicted to sensuality, he found it difficult to make a living. Recently, under the pretext of providing relief to the Northeast Volunteer Army, he had cards and receipts printed, falsely claiming to be a staff member of the relief team of that organization. He colluded with his friend Gao Xianchang, also from Anhui, to solicit donations from shops and residents in the Chinese area. He spent the funds and stayed in a room at the Dale Hotel at No. 6, Hongyuan Lane, Huade Road. At 7:20 AM the day before yesterday, Chinese constable Hao Yigu, detective Wu Shoushan, and Western constable Mai Kai of the Yulin Road police station went to the hotel to check for hidden bandits. They found Zhao's room, No. 35, and saw him in a flustered state. A small leather suitcase was placed on the bed. They asked him to open it. Zhao initially refused, but knowing that it was unavoidable, he opened it with trembling hands. Inside, they found five receipt books and a box of cards. When Constable Hao questioned him, Zhao suddenly became assertive and claimed that he was a staff member of a formal organization and that they should not interfere too much. The Chinese and Western detectives arrested him and took him, along with his friend Gao Xianchang and the suitcase, to the stairway of the hotel. Zhao, in desperation, knelt down and begged Constable Hao to release him, saying that he had been helping but failed. They were all detained in the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the previous situation and claimed that the first defendant, Zhao Yanru, claimed at the police station that he had an accomplice named Chen Zhonghe, who was indeed a staff member of the relief team and with whom he had contact. He had been fraudulently soliciting donations, totaling 130 yuan, from December last year to January this year. The money was all spent on a prostitute named Chen Juan in the French Concession. A photo of the prostitute has been copied. The victims included the Dafeng Coal Store at No. 595, Peng Road (2 yuan, with a receipt). The remaining cases will be investigated in detail. The police station has filed a public prosecution based on Article 364, Paragraph 1, of the Criminal Law for fraud and obtaining property. The second defendant, Gao Xianchang, is a well-known rogue on Huade Road and helped to defraud the money. If the two defendants were not caught, they would have gone to Suzhou to do the same thing. All the confiscated evidence will be submitted for inspection. Then, Chinese constable Hao Yigu and Chinese and Western detectives Jin Ming recounted the circumstances of arresting the two defendants. The owner of the Dafeng Coal Store on Peng Road, Wang Yongqing, testified that the defendant Zhao Yanru came to solicit a donation of 2 yuan on the 19th of this month and gave a receipt. When questioned, the two defendants stammered. After Judge Zhao Linyu verified the statements, he ordered them to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing for further investigation.

Father-in-law Sues Daughter-in-law for Abandonment

Zhu Zhongkan, a native of Ningbo, lived at Senyi Lane, Shanhai Pass Road, Shanghai. He married Wu Huilian, the daughter of Wu Xunqing, in 1931. In the late spring of last year, Zhongkan fell ill. Reader's Advisory

Further Discussion on "Production Rationalization" 152

｜Letter from Mr. Shen Yimin｜

Mr. Zhu Ying's reply to my previous letter discussing production rationalization (see this column, January 23rd) is fundamentally not

different. What Mr. Zhu is talking about is naturally the production rationalization of the current society, i.e., capitalist society. Its "result" will naturally "make you exhausted all day and unable to get enough to eat." The statement "This sentence can be established" is not a problem, and I did not object to it. The reason why I thought Mr. Zhu should explain it further is that some people, especially some laborers, often deeply resent and abhor the value of production rationalization itself because they suffer from the pain of capitalist production rationalization, and they do not have time to think about what significance this kind of experience of production rationalization has for the future socialist economic organization. Therefore, extending from Mr. Zhu's article is not entirely dissatisfaction with Mr. Zhu's words. Furthermore, in my opinion, what Mr. Zhu said today still has room for discussion: (1) Mr. Zhu said: "Mr. Shen's saying is based on 'the planned economy of the Soviet Union, which reveals this clue,' in other words, the economic organization of the Soviet Union also implements 'production rationalization.'" In fact, Mr. Zhu has misunderstood a bit. I only said that "the planned economy of the Soviet Union reveals this clue," and did not say that the Soviet Union has already implemented "production rationalization." (2) Mr. Zhu said: "Whether or not the Soviet Union seems to have reached this term, even if it is called 'production rationalization' in the future, the freedom and equality of capitalism and the freedom and equality of socialism are completely different.)" Yes, they are completely different. But this "completely different" is not in the institution of production rationalization, but in its social relations, in other words, in the purpose of socialist production rationalization, the subject of its application, and the scope of its application. I said very clearly in my previous letter: "...In this kind of society (i.e., socialist society, Yimin), production is no longer for the sake of commodities, but for the consumption of the producers themselves," and the editor of the Shanghai News reader's consultant said even more clearly in his reply: "...Production rationalization is the highest expression of the production method in a commodity-producing society, but when this highest production method reaches a certain level, it becomes incompatible with the production relations from which it came. As a result, it digs the grave for the social organization formed by this production relationship, and 'you all enter the bag, and then break out of his mother's womb and become the 'blessed child' of a higher stage of social organization.'" Therefore, I dare to say that the content of the Soviet Union's "Five-Year Plan" is the (higher expression) of the experience and technology of production rationalization in capitalist society, although it does not mark the term production rationalization, and although it has not fully expressed its content. As for the (term), it is a secondary issue. A newly established country on the road to socialism must use and learn the valuable experiences and technologies of bourgeois countries everywhere and inherit its great heritage in its entirety. For example, the democratic education and teaching methods of Dewey and Hall in the United States have one meaning in the capitalist society of the United States, but once they are adopted by the Soviet Union, they become completely another meaning. No one has ever denied that the Soviet Union has adopted American education methods because the Soviet Union has not marked democratic education. A researcher of materialist dialectics should pursue concrete problems, not just pursue the existence or absence of (terms). Because of Mr. Zhu's letter, I rashly expressed my opinions again. I hope Mr. Zhu and the readers will forgive my madness and foolishness and teach me. (Night of January 23rd)

Hangzhou Elementary School Teachers' Petition Results in the City Government Releasing All Educational Expenses 153

｜Totaling Over 40,000 Yuan｜

Teachers of municipal elementary schools in Hangzhou, due to the city government's financial difficulties, salary arrears for December have not been paid, and in view of the major closure period within the business community, requested advance payment of arrears and salary for January, and the seniority salary increase for the second semester of the 21st year and the first semester of the 22nd year be paid at the same time to show consideration. New China College (i.e., New China Public School) has been established for half a year and enjoys a good reputation. With the tireless planning of Principal Bai Wenwei and the school board, remarkable achievements have been made. A school board meeting was held on January 21st. In addition to the original appointments of Vice Principal Li concurrently as the director of the Political Science Department, Cui Shushi as the dean of the Business School and concurrently as the director of the General Business Department, Hu Yaochan as the dean of the Liberal Arts and Sciences School, Yuan Shuibo as the director of the Mathematics and Physics Department, Li Jianhua as the director of the Social Education Department, He Ziheng as the director of the Literature Department, Jiang Qitai as the director of the Economics Department, Hu Hanrui as the dean of academic affairs, Li Youlin as the secretary-general, Pan Danming as the director of student affairs, Hu Jun as the director of general affairs, and Yu Peng as the director of the middle school department, etc., the college has also newly hired Mr. Wei Jixi, the chief prosecutor of the Wuxing District Court, as the dean of the Law School and concurrently as the director of the Law Department. Currently, the school is raising funds to build school buildings and other development matters, and is scheduled to test new students on February 13th. The number of applicants is very large.

Cai Yuanpei Praises University and Middle School Entrance Examination Guidance 158

Students Taking Entrance Exams Should Not Miss This

Mr. Lu Shaoji, the director of the Normal Department of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School, has a considerable research in education. He has a very rich experience in guiding students to higher education. His recent books "University Entrance Examination Guidance" and "Middle School Entrance Examination Guidance" are noteworthy. "University Entrance Examination Guidance" explains the purpose, methods, procedures, and economic prospects of going to university and vocational schools, providing detailed guidance. It also collects the names, addresses, and content of universities and vocational schools across the country for selection. "Middle School Entrance Examination Guidance" guides elementary school students to enter middle school and middle school students to transfer schools. It provides detailed explanations of middle school education regulations, the content and nature of middle schools in various places, middle school expenses, examination rules and methods, and future prospects. The above two books were introduced by Mr. Cai Yuanpei to students across the country who are taking entrance exams to universities and middle schools, praising them as "indeed guidance for those who aspire to higher education." Therefore, we specially publish them for those taking entrance exams.

Preliminary Proposal for Reorganizing the National Normal School System (Part II) Luo Tingguang 159

3. Both normal schools and rural normal schools should be established independently. The length of study should be three years for normal schools and two or three years for rural normal schools (depending on local conditions). Both should enroll junior high school graduates. When necessary, rural normal schools may enroll senior elementary school graduates and provide them with a period of training.

4. In order to meet the needs of temporary teachers, normal schools may establish special normal departments and kindergarten normal departments, with a length of study ranging from one to two years.

5. Normal schools, rural normal schools, special normal departments, kindergarten normal departments, etc., should not charge tuition fees, and the government should provide food and lodging as a principle. Regarding the item of loan fees for normal school students, there are still many who disagree. They may say that normal schools are not charitable organizations after all, and the treatment of normal school students should not be different from that of ordinary middle school students, or that once normal schools are free, general poor students will flock to them, resulting in the loss of the original meaning of normal education, or that this will inevitably lead to the dependence of normal school students, etc. However, it is not known that normal education has a special purpose, so strict recruitment of new students to provide special training is also its fixed principle. The fact that normal schools do not charge tuition fees and that the government provides food and lodging as appropriate is one to show preferential treatment to normal school students, encourage them to study diligently, and strengthen their lifelong commitment to education, and the other is to strictly set standards to select suitable talents for training. This has achieved remarkable results in old normal schools. The state establishes political schools to train political workers, Party affairs schools to train Party affairs talents, and normal schools to train normal school talents. Political schools and Party affairs schools all achieve great results with free education. Why should there be doubts about free education for normal school students?

6. Normal universities and normal colleges of universities (i.e., current education colleges) are the orthodox institutions for cultivating secondary school teachers. In general, normal universities and normal colleges of universities have two missions: one is to cultivate secondary school teachers, and the other is to study education science. Otherwise, they are not worthy of the name of normal (university) and university (normal) (or (education)) college (Note 4). However, speaking separately, the two also have their differences. Normal universities are independently established institutions that can absolutely divide and train various teachers according to needs. Normal colleges of universities, because they are adjacent to other colleges, must earnestly connect with other colleges and cooperate to achieve the effect of division of labor. The detailed plan will be explained separately.

7. The establishment of normal schools should adopt a zoning system. Each province should be divided into several normal education zones according to actual conditions (Jiangsu is divided into six zones). Each zone should have at least one normal school. The whole country can also be divided into several higher normal education zones, each with at least one normal university or normal college of university. Normal schools or normal universities or normal colleges of universities, in addition to cultivating teachers, are also responsible for guiding and improving general education in their respective zones.

8. In order to meet the current urgent needs, normal universities and normal colleges of universities may establish advanced normal specialty departments, with a length of study of two or three years, to be determined according to actual conditions.

9. Normal universities, normal colleges of universities, and normal specialty departments do not charge tuition fees, and the government provides food and lodging as appropriate.

10. The service regulations for normal school students must be strictly stipulated. Those who do not comply will be disqualified and their expenses will be recovered. The reason why the service regulations for normal school students in the past were equivalent to mere formality was actually because the government authorities did not strictly implement them. In the future, efforts should be made to reform them, and they can be implemented in accordance with Article 6 of the Third Plenary Session Resolution (see above).

11. The future of normal school students should have a definite guarantee. Training should be carried out according to actual needs to ensure adequate supply so that normal school graduates have jobs to serve, or serve them to the best of their ability, or change their careers midway and leave. Various methods can be used (such as certifying teachers, improving teacher treatment, and guaranteeing education funding, etc.) to give them definite guarantees.

12. All levels of normal education institutions should have affiliated schools or experimental schools for normal school students to practice and research (Note 5).

13. The management and training of normal schools, normal universities, or normal colleges of universities should uniformly adopt strict principles, with the aim of cultivating teachers who are hardworking and able to endure hardship, love the country and love the group, and correcting the past accumulated malpractices of depression or selfishness.

14. Basic education and professional training should be equally emphasized in teaching. In addition to the educational knowledge they receive, normal school students should be roughly familiar with the content of the subjects they want to teach and be proficient in their teaching methods (Note 6).

15. Those who are not from a normal school background but want to be elementary and secondary school teachers must be certified and registered by the government. The regulations for certification and registration will be formulated separately.

(Note 1) In "The Advantages and Disadvantages of Merging Normal Schools and My Personal Opinions on This Issue" (China Education Circle, Volume 17, Issue 2), Luo Tingguang has investigated the reasons of all parties one by one, and ultimately does not approve of this system.

(Note 2) The full case can be found in the Shanghai News on January 27, 21.

(Note 3) See Charler W. Wand Wapleg Dy. The Qhmmonweath Teacher Training Stud: and Luo Tingguang, A New Theory of Normal Education (Nanjing), Chapter 8 for details.

(Note 4) See Luo Tingguang, The Problem of Normal Universities and University Education Colleges in the Midst of Educational Reform (Modern Education Monthly of Central University, Issue 1) for details.

(Note 5) See Luo Tingguang, A New Theory of Normal Education, Chapter 11 for details. (Note 6) Refer to the "Outline for Improving Normal Education in Jiangsu Province" promulgated by the Jiangsu Education Department.

Also refer to the First National Education Conference Report, the resolution on "Reorganizing the Normal Education System" and the original proposals.

Students should be well-prepared. Both books are 60 cents each, special price 10% off, postage 3 cents, registered mail add 8 cents, published by Quanfen Bookstore, 554 Sima Road, Shanghai.

Youth Turns Defeat into Victory; Jianhua and Huadong Victorious 162

Youth 37... Jianhua 33
