｜Eagle Team Expected to Have a Dramatic Battle Tonight｜

Last night at the Shanghai Basketball Association, the four group matches saw interest concentrated on the Youth vs. Jianhua game. Jianhua led for most of the way, seemingly smoothly, but unexpectedly, Youth was able to come from behind and turn defeat into victory. The Huadong vs. Xiaguang game lacked fixed formations and spirit, attracting few spectators and thus proving less exciting. Mei Gong vs. Liangxi, Group B1, 5:30 PM, Zhang Peter

The Jiangju vs. Mailing match on the 26th has been postponed. The Qingguang vs. Nanxing match on the 27th has been changed to February 1st at 8:30 PM.

Youth Turns Defeat into Victory In the second Group A1 match last night, Youth vs. Jianhua, the teams were evenly matched. Jianhua led most of the way, with Youth trailing behind. The Youth team is a combination of the Yohannan University and Middle School teams, and their movements were clean and crisp. In the first half, Jianhua won 17-13. In the second half, Youth still lagged behind. Despite intense attacks, there was no improvement. Furthermore, the pillar of their defense, Wu Youliang, was ejected for committing four fouls and replaced by Zhang Peixin. The situation suddenly improved. At that time, Jianhua still led by a score of 27-23. Youth surrounded and attacked, repeatedly probing the basket. Zhang Peixin and Tao Zunan repeatedly scored points. Cheng Jingxing and Zhou Xuexian made excellent corner shots, leveling and exceeding the score. Their momentum was immense. At this time, Jianhua's morale was greatly reduced. Focusing on strict defense, they turned victory into defeat, falling behind 29-35. Despite further efforts, they only added two points, and Youth ultimately turned defeat into victory by a margin of four points, with a final score of 37-33.

Huadong Wins with Difficulty The main event was the Group A match between Huadong and Xiaguang. Both sides had lost their inherent edge, with scattered formations and disordered advances and retreats, making the situation lax and greatly reducing interest. Huadong initially won 12-2. Xiaguang caught up, scoring five consecutive points to tie the score at 12-12. The situation became slightly tense, but the brilliance was still lacking. Huadong then regained momentum. Chen Xianglong and Xia Zeren scored 11 consecutive points. Yang Linyu also made a shot. At the end of the first half, Huadong led 26-15. The situation suddenly became tense in the second half, and the competition was fierce. Qian Dingshen of Huadong was unlucky, missing every shot. Xiaguang gradually caught up, exceeding Huadong twice with a score of 41-39. With little time remaining, Yang Linyu made a brilliant shot to tie the score at 41-41. In the ensuing scramble, with only four seconds left, it seemed like the game would end in a tie and go into overtime. However, Huadong had good fortune, and Chen Xianglong made a final shot to secure the victory, with a final score of 43-41.

Spring and Autumn

From Iron Birds to Sparrows 171

— Zhan Lu

Everyone knows that bomber planes, like soaring eagles, are the most terrifying things in the world. In the past year or two, the lives and properties of compatriots sacrificed under the enemy's iron birds, if totaled up, would be an astonishing record, a wound etched forever.

Iron birds are indeed terrifying, but the terror of sparrows is no less than that of iron birds! As the ancients said: "Three birds harm people: crows, bustards, and sparrows." In fact, the harm of opium and that of old bustards is not widespread. Among the three harms, only sparrows cause the greatest harm! In terms of the extent of their harm, they not only exceed crows and bustards, but also exceed bombers, which are called iron birds! This is because iron birds cause harm under special circumstances, while sparrows cause harm under widespread circumstances. The lives and properties sacrificed under iron birds are accidental, while the lives and properties sacrificed under sparrows are constant. Look! In ordinary families, it is difficult to find a copy of a national map; however, mahjong tiles are a common sight! Listen! In ordinary society, it is difficult to hear a few words that awaken the foolish and stubborn; in ordinary society, a few vivid and colorful mahjong gambling guides can be heard everywhere, whether on the streets, in alleys, in tea houses, or in taverns!

Some people say: Mahjong tiles have been exported and are popular in the New World. This shows that foreigners also like to play this game, so why blame only the people of this country? In fact, this is not the case. Americans play mahjong not as a form of gambling, but as a kind of group game. At banquets, mahjong games are organized according to the number of guests. After one game, the winners of each game are invited to form one or more games to compete in a rematch to determine the winner. Those who are eliminated for the first time can only watch from the sidelines and are not allowed to compete again. In this way, the winners continue to compete in the finals, and in the end, there must be one person who wins the championship. Focusing on the game and not betting on material things, how noble is that!

People only know that "oranges turn into trifoliate oranges when they cross the Huai River," but they do not know that "trifoliate oranges also turn into oranges when they cross the Huai River." Mahjong is not a noble game, but when it flies to America, it becomes noble. Isn't this the trifoliate orange turning into an orange when it crosses the Huai River?

Opium Comedy 172

— Luo Cunren

｜What happened after public sales｜

If opium were a religion, and we compared the followers of other religions with the followers of this opium religion, I think the great religions of the world would have to come to our Chinese opium religion. Look at how many missionaries and believers there are! Take my hometown as an example. There are only forty or fifty households, but there are four or five opium dens. I saw the following with my own eyes:

A husband, as if losing his soul, shouted to his wife: "Where did you hide the opium I just bought? Bring it here quickly!" The wife pleaded: "Leave it for me to enjoy! I haven't had any for days."

At this time, their anemic four-year-old boy was so hungry that he could not move. He gestured for his mother to fetch mud and cook rice in the pot.

The poor uncle next door heard his nephew and niece-in-law quarreling, came over and scolded them, and confiscated all their opium paraphernalia and opium to show his punishment.

The uncle took his nephew's opium home and smoked it behind closed doors, because he was also an old addict who had no money to buy it. Alas! Opium's China!

Songs and Children 173

— Zhong Yan

｜A Warning to Parents｜

Good songs can imperceptibly improve children's temperament, and bad songs can also imperceptibly worsen children's temperament. Songs have a very important relationship with children, so parents must choose and correct the songs that children can come into contact with.

There are many good songs, but there are also quite a few bad ones. In my county (Fushan, Shandong), there is a very popular song:

Little fat boy, climbs on the windowsill, steals his father's (1) silver dollars; his father beats him, his mother pulls (2) him.

If a child learns to sing this kind of song from a young age, he will get the impression of stealing in his mind. How can he become a good citizen in the future? I am afraid that there are such songs everywhere, so I advise parents not to ignore them.

(1) Father, (2) pleading on his behalf.

The Roll-aways of Society 174

— Tian Fang

Near where I live, there is an old temple inhabited by several ascetic monks. Every early morning, the rhythmic sound of the wooden fish, "ge ge," reaches your pillow, often causing me to imagine their lives with pity. These pitiful selfish people have all been fooled by Indian black charcoal, full of the hope of becoming immortals or Buddhas and ascending to heaven in broad daylight, yet they are still burdened by a stinking skin that needs the support of human material offerings. In the end, when they close their eyes, a mound of yellow earth. Let others name becoming immortals and Buddhas. Isn't the end of life the same as ordinary people? What is the difference between "studying Buddhism" and "waiting to die"? If it is said to be praying to be reborn in the Western Paradise, but if they knew that the "India" they seek is the hometown of the red-headed Indians, that honey bee's needle

During the great battle at the Nine Gates, the campus beauties of Beiping's universities were still ice skating and skiing, enjoying their timely pleasure. Their behavior is probably even worse than the singing girls of the Hou Ting Hua.

When a person's dog goes missing, they want to publish a notice to find it. When a Japanese dog is stolen, they want to hold a memorial service. In the past, in foreign parks, (Chinese and dogs) were treated equally, but now it seems that some people are not as good as dogs.

The French Concession's Gujia Garden is called (Gujia Garden) by the concession authorities, but the people of Shanghai unanimously call it (French Park). This is just like calling the British Concession the Great British Territory, which makes people who come to Shanghai feel jarred! (Sha Yu)

"(Second Master is back)," Hongye's nephew stood at the door.

Hongye didn't have time to answer, and hurried inside. Stepping over the threshold, his father was lying on a rattan couch in the hall. His thin cheeks, a head of long, messy white hair, which had not been trimmed for a long time, looked even more haggard. He wasn't wearing socks, and his feet seemed to be swollen to the point of bursting. His hands and cheeks were also swollen. When he saw Hongye coming in, a smile appeared on his face.

"(Ah! Hongye has come back to see me)!"

"(Dad...)"

His throat locked up, and he couldn't say a second word. His mother and brother led him into the room and told him in a low voice that the doctors in the city were already out of options. Yesterday, someone recommended Doctor X, who was a very famous doctor in Y County, to come to C City for a consultation, which would cost 100 yuan. Without a big favor, he might not even be willing to come. Today, at dawn, the foreman was sent to take a note from Old Zhang next door and take the long-distance bus to ask him to come. He wondered if he would give them the honor.

Hongye also knew that since his father had returned home, almost all of the famous doctors in C Township had been consulted in turn. After taking each doctor's virgin prescription, his sleep was usually more peaceful at night, and the swelling was slightly reduced. However, after taking three or four doses of medicine, he would return to his original state. The famous doctors in C Township were very gentlemanly. If they couldn't cure the disease themselves, they would recommend a worthy person to replace them. A would recommend B, and B would recommend C. The last Confucian doctor, having truly been unable to recommend a doctor who hadn't seen his father's illness before, sighed and frowned, holding Hongye's brother's hand, as if he was about to cut off a piece of his own flesh. "(Your father's illness, his heart's blood has dried up, and I am afraid it cannot be recovered by human power. Tonight, I will respectfully invite the Buddha to descend to the altar and judge the good or bad fortune for you. You yourself can kneel before the altar and ask)."

Hongye's brother, trembling with fear, crawled before the altar and kowtowed three times. The altar's message was the four words "(Life has ended)." That Confucian doctor then left without explanation and never came again.

When eating lunch, his father was still lying on the rattan couch. Suddenly, he pointed to the grilled shrimp on the table; "(The fish and shrimp here cannot be eaten elsewhere, Hongye, you can eat more)." Hongye, who had been under his strict father's knee for twenty years, had never heard this kind of loving tone before. It was like a bright silver needle piercing deep into his heart! Besides saying "(Ah)," he couldn't eat any more. The C Township creed was swirling in his mind:

"(People who are sick should not change their temper)."

Three sedan chair bearers, chanting, actually brought the famous Doctor X from Y County. Hongye followed his brother, dressed in formal attire, to greet him into the study. He turned out to be a short man with a black beard and crossed legs. After looking, asking, feeling the pulse, he picked up a pen and wrote out a pulse diagnosis in one breath on seven or eight sheets of flowered stationery. He was truly like a thousand words written while leaning on a horse, as if he had innate wisdom.

"(Amitabha! This doctor must be your father's savior! Where have you ever heard of a prescription being written on seven or eight sheets of stationery)?" His mother heard Hongye's report, adding one sheet after another. It was only on the eleventh and a half sheet that the taste of joy came. The first ingredient was a pair of clams.

"(I'm afraid this clam cannot be found in the small pharmacies here, you have to go to Richeng to buy it)." (Four)

Zhe Yu Yi

Statements from a Snow-Viewing Spectator 175

— Lin Heng

The wind is as sharp as a blade, the snow as large as goose feathers. The poor rush about with cold stomachs, the rich enjoy the snow around a warm brazier.

The rich sit in Western-style houses with hot water radiators, warm as spring. They look at the snowy scenery through glass windows, so leisurely, so interesting! When they go out, they add a fur coat on top of their fur robes, and sit in sedan-style cars. The northwest wind can't even move a hair on their heads!

I am not rich, so of course I don't have the privilege of living in a Western house or riding in a car. On Avenue Joffre, which seems endless, pedestrians are as rare as morning stars. I stood at the intersection of Rue Pichon, braving the wind and snow, and after waiting for more than a quarter of an hour, a tram finally passed from west to east. I dared not delay, and as soon as the tram stopped, I jumped into the third-class carriage. There were very few people in the carriage, and it was easy to find a seat. As soon as I sat down, I suddenly heard someone shout: "Old Lin! Where are you going?" I looked closely and saw that it was my classmate, Mr. Chen, a movie buff. I replied: "I'm going to a friend's house on Avenue Hua Lung. Where are you going at this hour?" Mr. Chen said: "I'm going to see a movie." I said: "Now the Northeast Volunteer Army is braving the snow to resist Japan, and you are in the mood to brave the snow to see a movie?" Mr. Chen said: "Don't satirize me. Although movies are a form of entertainment, meaningful movies are very beneficial to social education, like '(Two Daughters of the Northeast)' abandoning personal feelings and going to the national crisis; '(A Double Tragedy in a Sea of Sin)' breaking the inheritance system and advocating that the rich use their wealth to organize public welfare. If our Chinese compatriots could all be like the two daughters in '(Two Daughters of the Northeast)' and the rich man in '(A Double Tragedy in a Sea of Sin),' I'm afraid the Northeast Volunteer Army would have already recovered the lost territories." I said: "Alright, alright! I suppose you have a reason for seeing movies. But what about those of us who don't have money to see movies?" At this moment, the tram had arrived at the Hua Long Road station, and I said goodbye to Mr. Chen! and hastily got off the tram.

On Western Opera 176

I myself don't know much about Western opera. But I have generally discussed or know about those famous ancient scripts. However, in Shanghai, even though it is considered the Paris of the East, it is not easy to see Western opera performed on stage on the western shore of the Pacific Ocean. In reality, the Chinese people fundamentally do not need these arts, and they may not even understand them. Even the Westerners traveling in China are mostly fat-bellied compradors of foreign firms, or pastors in churches, who may not truly understand the (essence) of opera. Verdi's "(La) Traviata" ... Moreover, when Western opera is occasionally performed in Shanghai, it is only by Italian troupes traveling the world, who perform for a week or two and then leave. They use the Italian language, singing dialogues and poems. Not to mention that Chinese people can easily understand it, even the English and French who interpret it with English translations cannot obtain the rich emotional tones within the play. ... Even full-fledged Italians rarely have appreciative confidants.

However, for the past few days, the Carlton Theatre has been performing world-famous plays by the "(San) Carlo Opera Company." Not because of the reasons above, the theater is not (empty enough to catch sparrows), but rather business is booming, giving the impression of (an audience filled with appreciative listeners). There, people of all countries and ethnicities are present, as can be seen from their actions and clothing; even many Chinese men and women. | I will not hesitate to admit that I also went with the musician Hu Jingxi to appreciate La Boheme (transliterated as Pohanmi, meaning romantic or wandering artists) by Murger a hundred years ago.

It is only a simple tragic scene about artists' tragic love in a life of poverty. It is divided into four acts: ㈠ Paris in 1830 ㈡ Cafe Momus in Paris ㈢ The gates of Paris ㈣ Same as the first act. In this, just like a Jiangnan person who has never practiced Peking opera listening to Mei Lanfang's fast-paced opera with unfamiliar tones, I do not understand the Italian language. But from their voices, actions, and expressions, I understand it as clearly as if I were watching a shadow play, especially because the accompanying music gives many hints, I can very comfortably experience the script of La Boheme that I have read. (End)

Then he would definitely not want to be born in India to be a descendant of a subjugated people. Putting everything aside, regardless of whether immortals or Buddhas exist, even if they ascend to heaven in broad daylight and attain permanent Nirvana, if they are not absurd stories, then from (birth) to (Nirvana) (ascension), all the processes of going to immortals and Buddhas cannot but require the support of the human world. By the time (merit and practice are complete), they become immortals and Buddhas, but they do not recognize their parents, do not acknowledge their relatives, and even more so do not acknowledge the farmers and workers who clothe and feed me, and the teachers and friends who teach me. This is called (each one cultivates and each one attains), abandoning all affection, isn't that a huge escapee from society? Fortunately, my Buddha is not effective, and not everyone is fooled. To this day, the human race is still diverse and has no worries about food and clothing, and the world has not been occupied by wild beasts. Otherwise, wouldn't the term (humanity) have long been extinct?

Writing this article is to advise those who are stepping on the earth but whose souls are flying beyond the heavens.

Silk and Tea: The London Tea Market Plummets 181

According to news from British merchant firms, the tea market in London has been extremely sluggish recently. Retrospect of the Yarn Flower Market in the Past Year (II) 182

The sales market for native yarn also promotes spring sales. The Cantonese people have a strong sense of patriotism and are actively involved in handling native yarn. Many other ports also participate. According to statistics, this port exported 44,182 bales of cotton yarn in January, 19,690 bales in February, and 8,526 bales in March. The outbreak of war in February and March caused a sharp decline in exports. Although the Shanghai battle had ceased in the summer, the domestic economy was bankrupt and the silk industry was declining, resulting in weak demand. In addition, the financial sector cautiously released loans, concentrating silver dollars in Shanghai, causing the foreign exchange rate to fall to within 70 cents (approximately 68 cents). Since inland sales were denominated in foreign currency, while Shanghai sales were usually in taels of silver, the price of each yarn piece was implicitly reduced by about one or two taels of silver. This situation was very unfavorable for yarn sales, and yarn prices also suffered a discount due to actual sales, leading to a drop in prices. The yarn exports for April were 12,433 bales, 44,885 bales in May (yarn market opening), and 19,592 bales in June. Since the autumn season, due to the adverse weather conditions for American cotton, the Bureau of Agriculture had theories of hoarding and insect pests. The Cantonese merchants first searched the market as much as possible, and pre-purchased yarn for the months of August, September, October, November, and December. As a result, the market was stimulated and prices soared. The spot price of 20-count "Ren Zhong" yarn rose from 152 taels to 164 taels and 5 mace. In one month, the spot transaction volume reached a huge 80,312 bales, setting the highest transaction record of the year. Afterwards, the market entered a calm state. In August, exports were only 27,869 bales, and in September, 23,427 bales. Japanese merchants resumed dumping tactics, competing for sales at low prices in the Yangtze River region. 20-count yarn was often more than ten taels cheaper per piece, and 42-count yarn was more than twenty or thirty taels lower. The north was the first to be invaded by them. Those who transported native yarn to the north were all occupied by Japanese merchants, leaving no room for insertion. Tianjin had a large amount of yarn in stock, and urgently sought a way out, even selling in Shanghai. In addition, American cotton also experienced a sharp price drop, and civil strife broke out in Shandong Province. Sichuan was originally a major sales area for our country's yarn, but unexpectedly, the two Liu's suddenly engaged in a fierce battle, the impact of which need not be stated. Exports were 24,709 bales in October, 22,789 bales in November, and 14,123 bales in December. The total transaction volume for the year was 362,482 bales, a decrease of 177,583 bales compared to the previous year. It is observed that the Shanghai cotton yarn firm industry is gradually being eliminated. Since the establishment of the exchange, all the achievements of the yarn market have been attributed to the futures market. Therefore, the power of yarn firms has been declining. For example, the retail stores in the Nanshi district and the wholesale yarn firms north of the Suzhou River have extremely limited business. Therefore, there are few new yarn firms established in recent years. Yarn factories such as Shenxin and Wing On see foreign yarn rampant in various provinces. In order to seek a way out, they have set up distribution and wholesale offices in major yarn sales areas across the country to compete with foreign yarn. There is also China Textile Corporation, which buys cotton and sells yarn at cotton producing ports in various provinces. The company is like the Japanese merchant's Dongmian Corporation. In addition, the larger yarn firms with larger import and export volumes, such as Yida and Fuji Hongxing, are all attached to the exchange (the yarn firms of various groups have been recorded in previous reports). Talks

The Art of Not Asking 194

— Fearless

That day, after hearing the phrase "(If you want to eat squid, don't ask)" in a provisions store, I savored the words "(don't ask)" and felt that these three words are a kind of art of living.

"(Don't ask)" means "(Don't meddle in other people's business)". Indeed, one should pretend to be ignorant and deaf, and it's best to eat more and talk less in these times.

The so-called XX groups, etc., have now melted away, but not long ago, didn't these kinds of groups warn merchants in the east and throw bombs in the west? But the treacherous merchants are still stocking up, and the import of enemy goods along the Yangtze River is still increasing, while the passionate youths who did these things are already caught in the net of the law. Therefore, passionate youths, you should try your best to suppress your passion! Embrace the principle of "(Don't listen, don't ask)". It is most carefree, and those who worry about the country and grieve about the times are fools. In short, just eat, don't talk, don't listen, don't ask, no matter if the Japanese invade Rehe or Peiping-Tientsin, or even Nanjing, don't care. If people ask you why you are indifferent, you can just answer like this: We have a government in place, and the government is still calmly believing in the League of Nations. What business is it of us ordinary people to meddle in? The emperor isn't worried, but the eunuch is getting anxious.

Recently, supervising committee member X impeached so-and-so, which caused some questioning, etc. It's really looking for trouble for no reason. Perhaps committee member X doesn't understand this art of living?

Moreover, if you ask about everything carefully, it's truly annoying. A murder case may have many hidden backgrounds, and it's just that you hide it from me, and I hide it from you. If you don't know what's good for you and you go ask and meddle, you're sure to be rebuffed.

For example, when going to a foreign goods store to buy cloth, just buy it if the price is low and the quality is good. If you ask in detail, the result you get may not be satisfactory. Instead, you might encounter a "top" (we don't sell non-domestic goods), and maybe you'll see the clerk's awkward face. Your conscience will be pricked, and then you won't be able to buy cheap goods.

Therefore, in conclusion, the first thing to say is "(Don't ask!)" Friends! Are you willing to learn this art of living? However, although I write it, I hope that no one will want to learn this art, that's not against my true intention.

Literature & Art

Year-End Musings 195

— Li Tangzhu

Severe cold, wind, rain, and snow spread, year after year, the year ends again. Looking up at the mountains and rivers, I grieve for the chaotic world, indeed, advancing or retreating is always difficult.

The country is like a melon, divided by powerful figures. The sores and wounds are all caused by the three dukes. Stealing life makes one envy the soldiers, dying on the battlefield is a good end.

The sound of the flute arises everywhere with sad songs, brave men march far away, pillows on spears at night. They fight to throw their heads once, relying on iron and blood to restore the country.

Ashamed to hide in the utopian Peach Blossom Spring, though survival is good, it's lamentable to be passive. Lying on firewood still performs demonic dances, saddened that my divine land is full of drunken people. (In response to assisting the righteous army)

Science

Manufacturing Methods of Artificial Rubber 196

— Erming

Nowadays, there is no one who does not know what rubber is used for. This is because rubber has a soft and not easily damaged characteristic. Therefore, quite a few of our daily necessities are made of rubber. However, the demand for rubber products is very small, and the natural rubber is enough to supply the application. Until the production of automobiles, the wheels are all made of rubber. Therefore, the demand for rubber has increased rapidly, and the natural products are not enough to supply people's needs. So, a general scientist stood up to study artificial rubber to supplement the insufficiency of natural products and meet the needs of human beings. Now artificial rubber is popular in the world, but there are very few people who know how to make it. Therefore, the important ones are described below for the purpose of popularization. Those who are interested in research may also wish to check special manufacturing books to understand the mystery.

To make artificial rubber compete with natural rubber,

The value of the manufactured artificial rubber must be cheaper than natural rubber, and its quality is equal to or better than it. To solve all kinds of problems, one must start by studying the raw materials for manufacturing artificial rubber. Now, limited to space, I am sorry that I cannot describe it.

The most important raw material for manufacturing artificial rubber is Isoprene, but carbon oxides similar to this, such as Butadiene, a tetracarbon diene, can also be used. The method of manufacturing artificial rubber is nothing more than polymerizing Isoprene. The method is nothing more than placing Isopene or other raw materials in a sealed dish and warming it to a considerable amount of time to make rubber. The height of the temperature should vary depending on the raw materials used.

㈠ Manufacturing with Petroleum Spirit. Take an appropriate amount of petroleum spirit (petroleum spirit contains pentane) and use it to combine with oxygen to synthesize pentyl chloride. Then contact the pentyl chloride with roasted lime to remove hydrogen chloride. Then mix the obtained hydrocarbon pentene with oxygen chloride. The chemical reaction that occurs is only one trimethyl ethylene is separated, then it becomes 2-methyl-2-chlorobutane. If chlorinated again, 2-methyl-2,4-dioxy-tetracarbon alkane (2M) and 2-methyl-2,3-dichlorobutane (2M) are obtained. Add alkali lime to the last two compounds obtained to obtain Isoprene.

㈡ Manufacture with starch. First dissolve the starch in boiling water to gelatinize it, and then ferment it to form a mixture of normal butyl alcohol and acetone. Then use distillation to separate the acetone and add oxygen chloride to the normal tetracarbon alcohol to turn it into butyl chloride. Then add chlorine and oxygen to become 3,4-

Page 20

Tetracarbon alkane (1,4-dichlorobutane), its boiling point is extremely low, if it is passed through red-hot alkali lime, it will immediately turn into a tetracarbon diene. Tetracarbon diene is extremely easy to gasify, so it must be cooled to become a liquid. The method is to use solidified carbon dioxide and ether to protect the outside of the condenser. Once tetracarbon diene is obtained, methylchliride is used to compound it and Isoprene is formed. Although the rubber obtained by this method cannot be completely different from natural rubber, its quality is actually better.

(Three) Manufacturing with coal. Place coal and lime in an electric furnace and burn it to obtain calcium carbide. When calcium carbide is added to water, Acetylene gas is immediately released. If acetylene is combined with water and mercuric chloride is used as an accelerator, Acetaldehyde can be formed. Oxidation will turn it into acetic acid. Acetic acid and Sodium Soanride undergo a chemical reaction to become Sodium Acetone. Adding tetracarbon acetylene gas to copper ketonide can obtain Metfylbutiol. Changing Methylbutiol to Methylbutenol, contact the final methylbutenol obtained with Magnesium Sulfate to produce sopeneo.

㈣ Manufacturing with wood chips. Dry distill the wood chips to obtain the acetone contained therein, and then use a pot to change it into aluminum salt and IsoProPenol. Hydration yields aluminum and Pinacol. Removing two water molecules from Pinacol can yield Dimethyl Butadiene. Polymerizing dimethyl tetracarbon diene yields rubber. Fermenting sweet potatoes to produce acetone is also often used.

The manufacturing of Methylrubber W is to place liquid dimethyl tetracarbon diene in a double-walled dish and raise the temperature to 70 degrees Celsius. After five months, the dimethyl tetracarbon diene contained in the dish will turn into a solid, greenish-yellow rubber. W is the abbreviation of German Weib, which means soft. This type of artificial rubber is suitable for manufacturing soft utensils.

Methylrubber H is named for its hardness. Its manufacturing method is also to store dimethyl tetracarbon ene in a thin-walled tin dish, and then raise the temperature to 30 degrees Celsius. After three months, a white, porous coagulum is formed. This kind of rubber is very different from natural rubber, but its use is very large.

Snow Sledding 197

—

"Hey! Old Zhang! The whole back playground is frozen and icy. Let's go play ball on the snow," Old Chen, who never liked playing ball, suddenly became excited today. He automatically took off his silk cotton robe and called out to Old Zhang, who was sitting at his desk preparing for chemistry.

"Okay, anyway, there's no exam tomorrow."

They excitedly came to the back playground and saw that Old Cheng, Old Tan, and others were already playing vigorously.

"Oh! I really can't take it, I've slipped five or six times," Old Tan said as soon as he saw them, opening his dog mouth and barking wildly. Originally, Old Tan's nickname was Ah Huang.

"I think it's okay not to play ball, but what should we play? Skating without shoes," Old Chen changed his original intention.

At that time, Old Zhang discovered something and shouted wildly: it was a broken desk, lying upside down on the snow.

"Come on! Let's push a snow sled, I haven't played this for many years."

"Okay," Old Cheng hurried to the dormitory upstairs and took the rope for tying luggage.

Everyone worked together, and finally the snow sled was completed. "How interesting! An uncultured person is sitting on the snow sled with peace of mind," this was said by Old Chen five minutes later while sitting on the sled. At the same time, Old Cheng was carrying it with a rope in front, Old Zhang and Old Tan were pushing in the back, and several other classmates were laughing beside them.

But happiness always leads to sorrow, the annoying disciplinarian came.

"Hey! Why are you destroying public property?" The disciplinarian walked over, grabbed the rope, and insisted on calling them to the disciplinary office together.

"What are you talking about? The desk was already broken," Old Chen, feeling wronged, jumped off the desk first and negotiated with the disciplinarian.

"Why do you want to pull my rope? This is not from the school." Old Cheng has always been

"I want you to go to the disciplinary office," the disciplinarian was unwilling to show weakness.

"We'll pay for your desk, how much? Put it on our account, anyway, each of us has two yuan of compensation reserve," Old Tan was also angry.

"Go to the disciplinary office? I'll go with you," Old Zhang said.

"I want you to put down the rope," Old Cheng used the strength of an ox to snatch the rope from the disciplinarian's hand.

"Are you guys dare to hit someone?" The disciplinarian was simply helpless and said this to save face. "We want to hit you? It's okay to go to the disciplinary office," instead, Old Zhang wanted to go.

When they arrived at the disciplinary office, the disciplinary director felt that it would be very embarrassing to give them a demerit because they were students with high grades. As a result, they were lectured, and the four people jointly compensated for the desk, which totaled six yuan.

Winter vacation has begun, and everyone received a warning letter. They laughed and said: This is the reward for pushing the snow sled, a fearless person, at this point, his hair stood on end in anger.

How is the Power? 198

— Written by Guanghuan

Chrysanthemum Tea 199

— Flood

"It's very clean here, please sit down." The resourceful waitress Wang in the XX Theater saw two young tourists approaching and hurriedly greeted them.

"Please sit down, gentlemen!" Her words stopped, followed by her flexible eyes darting a glance at them and showing a smug smile. She used her soft fingers to gently push them on their shoulders, sending them into the chairs. Lu, who embraced hedonism, took advantage of the situation and slid into the chair; he couldn't help but laugh loudly and roughly. "Tea? Black tea, green tea, or chrysanthemum tea?" "Don't want any tea." Zhuang had suffered a loss in the amusement park once, and he knew that the place was full of scams. Even if you drink a cup of the cheapest plain water, you will be charged two cents.

"Do you like chrysanthemum tea? Oh, sir, wipe your face!" She finally brought two cups of chrysanthemum tea and squeezed out two hot towels.

"Sir, please help, you don't care about spending a few dollars, thank you." She warmly entertained them. She had wavy hair, shiny black eyes, a peach-colored face, and rosy lips, all of which could ignite Lu's heart. So he mustered all his courage and started chatting with her.

"How much business can you do in a day?"

"Quite a bit, we can sell hundreds of cups of tea in a day, but we have to split it with the accounting department."

"Oh! We can earn five or six yuan a day."

"It's very hard work, busy day and night."

"Then why don't you look for a better job?"

"That's right. Sir, if I abandon my current job, how can I maintain my life? Can society give us a better job? Of course, that's another question. Especially in today's society, it's even more difficult for women to find jobs."

"What's your real motivation for coming here? I want to ask blindly."

"To be honest! My hometown is far away in Shenyang. When the September 18th Incident first started, our officers did not resist and offered the land || that is, our hometown, to the violent Japanese with both hands. So I fled to Shanghai with my old mother. My younger brother, seeing that the lost land has not been recovered, wants to win back a bit of personality for our nation, and has already joined the righteous army!" Her attitude was very angry and tragic. "Speaking of which, because I can't leave my rice-wasting mouth idle, I have exhausted my relatives and friends and tried every means to keep my job here." Zhuang heard her words, especially the sentence "(He wants to win back a bit of personality for our nation)", and he suddenly felt ashamed and without a place to stand. He thought, Yuguan has now fallen, and Japan is urgently occupying Rehe, which is also in a serious state. Recalling the loyal and brave volunteers in the Northeast, they are fighting a desperate battle with the violent Japanese in the icy and snowy land. They have no warm clothes to wear, no reinforcements... So a nameless sadness arose in his heart again! He, Zhuang, no longer had the heart to listen to the opera, and pulled Lu's clothes angrily and said:

"Go back! Pay for the two cups of chrysanthemum tea and go back!"

They left the noisy amusement park and went down from the cage-like elevator.

Skinning a Pig? Or Donating on Behalf of 200

— Jin Huan

On a snowy night, there were no people on the road, only the cutting cold wind, fluttering goose-feather-like white snow, shrouded around me. At this time, I braved the wind and snow, courageously moving forward, while admiring the dignitaries and wealthy people, who were warming themselves by the fire.

"Friend! Friend!" These two short and urgent sounds suddenly stunned me. Looking closely, I suddenly found a big man blocking my way, and several heroic figures also窜ed out of a dark and narrow alley next to me. My heart suddenly became anxious, but then calmed down, preparing to be pig-skinned once! "Friend: Be sensible!" a young man in an overcoat said to me!

"Friend: Since you are a friend, please help me!" I answered like this:

"What! I want you to be sensible, but you want me to help you!"

"I'm sorry! The robe is borrowed, and you can take the four cents in my pocket to buy a cigarette."

"Joke: You underestimate us too much, we are not thugs!"

"What joke! I really don't have money!"

"Don't pretend to be stupid, we're going to be rude!"

"Friend, then wait for me to untie it and let you search, okay?"

"Joke! What do you take us for? To be honest: don't get the wrong idea, this is not for us to use!" Then who is it for?

"Haha: I'm donating on behalf of the Northeast Volunteer Army!"

"Then I've donated several times already!"

"Sir, you are enthusiastic and patriotic, please spend some money this time!"

Before long, the hat, scarf, robe, and watch were all transferred in one breath in the midst of enthusiastic patriotic voices, and everyone dispersed in a hoot of laughter, saying "(Come and get the receipt tomorrow)!"

Clerk Communication

The Stepmother Problem (II) 201

Dear Editor: Since the birth of (Clerk Communication), I have wanted to raise my question and ask for your advice; but because of my lack of talent and knowledge, I did not have the courage to write. Finally, the desire for knowledge overcame my shame. Today, I will write this letter to you shamelessly: If there are any incomprehensible or wrong characters, I hope you will forgive me for being a person who has not even graduated from elementary school, and give me corrections.

I am twenty years old this year, and logically it is an era of striving for progress: but because of the influence of a bad family and the oppression of a bad environment, I have to be pessimistic and negative.

My loving mother passed away ten years ago; the subsequent stepmother was extremely fierce. I can't bear to recount the suffering I suffered in my childhood. Now, although she faces me with a crying face, she is secretly trying to arrange me!

Men should marry and women should marry when they are old enough, which is of course the inevitable path in life. Unexpectedly, she came up with a strange idea and insisted that I marry her niece. Generally speaking, cousins becoming husband and wife is the best thing; but she advocates this saying, but there is another effect in it! She has now given birth to four children, the oldest of whom is only five years old: seeing that my father, who is over sixty years old, cannot always protect them, she came up with this method to bind me.

Now her family is very good, and my maternal uncle and others have a lot of face in Shanghai; my current business is all in their hands. She expects that I dare not be willful with the rice bowl, so she insists on her ghost plan; she is afraid that if I marry another woman, I will not be able to cooperate with her, and if the woman's family is also powerful, then my business may not depend on her brother.

Now I want to break away from the scope of the family and maternal uncle, etc., but in this snobbish society, the future is also very bleak: in case I fail to find a job, wouldn't I become (want to be successful, but can't be successful)? Sir, in my situation, is it better to endure it? Or is it better to find a way out? I hope you can give me guidance as soon as possible. (The following is omitted) Respectfully, Yu Kunfu.

···············

Editor's note; Yu Jun's letter, at first glance, seems to include two issues, marriage and career choice. But after detailed research, the reason why he refuses to marry his cousin, and is eager to break away from his maternal uncle, is nothing more than to get rid of his stepmother's control, so this is purely a stepmother problem.

When Yu Jun's biological mother abandoned her, his father was already over fifty years old, and Yu Jun was only ten years old. If his stepmother had not come to take charge of the family affairs, then his father would not have been able to take care of both his career and his children; if he had taken care of his children, he would not have been able to take care of his career. We have to recognize that she is a contributor to Yu Jun's family. A chicken's skin cannot be glued to a duck's body. Although Yu Jun cannot treat her as his own mother, he cannot treat her as a stranger after all. Now she is seeking perfection for the sake of future livelihood, and her heart is also very bitter. The way of Confucius is loyalty, Yu Jun also seems to should let go of his previous grievances and treat her with courtesy in order to please his father. As for the marriage issue, Yu Jun certainly has the right to decide for himself, but it must be based on the other party's character and knowledge, and there must be no other prejudice mixed in. We also believe that if he can marry the niece of this stepmother, it can also avoid the general conflicts between mothers-in-law and daughters-in-law seen in society, which may not be Yu Jun's lifelong blessing.

As for finding another job, then it should be determined based on whether there is hope in the current position. Moreover, for the sake of prudence, it is best to adopt the method of (riding a horse while looking for another horse to ride). There is no need to hold the concept of (cannot live here for a day) simply because the current position was recommended by the stepmother's brother.

Westerners have a proverb that says (everything looks blue when viewed through blue glasses). Yu Jun's view of his stepmother may also be in this situation; therefore, he feels that everything about his stepmother, and even everything that is slightly related to his stepmother, is more terrifying than poisonous snakes and fierce tigers. I hope you can quickly remove these blue glasses and get along with your stepmother in a calm and peaceful manner.

Novel

A Literate Family (5th continuation) 202

— Wang Zhongxian

㈢ Having her can really prolong life by a few years

Miss Daiqiu | Ruohua's daughter | unknowingly followed her to Xia's family as a dowry. Because Xia Zhongnan had no biological son, she took the Xia surname. The girl grew up smart and lively. Except for Mrs. Xia, the whole family liked her very much. Zhongnan loved her like a pearl in his palm. After entering the door, he immediately sent her to school until Zhongnan stepped down and returned to his hometown, just leaving school life.

Zhongnan's first wife! Her temperament is stubborn, and her heart is narrow. She is completely a typical old-fashioned woman. She originally had a liver pain problem, and when it flared up severely, she would faint from the pain. In the past, she only fell ill once or twice a year, but since Ruohua entered the door, the number of times she fell ill has gradually increased - although Zhongnan and Ruohua did not dare to invade her, she imagined the annoyance herself.

Zhongnan pampered that stepdaughter, and Mrs. Xia was also very jealous when she saw it, often scolding her as a bastard in front of the servants. In front of the first wife, the servants were only allowed to call Daiqiu's name, and no one was allowed to call her Miss. Maosheng was not liked by the first wife, but in order to compete with Daiqiu, she deliberately showed her love and praised him extremely highly. Using this pair of children, she could vent her anger and insult Ruohua. Ruohua wanted to resist many times, but Zhongnan restrained her.

The first wife praised Maosheng to suppress Daiqiu, but Maosheng was an unpromising thing: not only was he not as smart as Daiqiu in studying, but he also often did many nasty things, making the servants look down on him. The first wife was also often angered by this son and developed liver and stomach problems.

The fifth master followed his brother in reading while in office. Ruohua knew that Zhongnan loved this younger brother the most, so she treated him especially warmly, caring for him in every way. The fifth master was very grateful in his heart and said to Ruohua in front of his brother:

(The eldest sister-in-law is like a mother, and the second sister-in-law is not the eldest sister-in-law, but her heart in caring for me is really the same as my loving mother.)

(Fifth brother's words are really killing me! We are all one family, and we are also far away from home, so we should take care of each other. You are young and studying hard outside. In the future, if you are successful, it will also be the glory of our Xia family. If the elder brothers and sisters-in-law don't take care of you, do we teach outsiders to take care of you? Fifth brother's polite words are not like one of our own!)

(Having her, ah...) Zhongnan sat on the sofa and said to Youzhong with a smile; (Having her can really prolong life by a few years. I don't have to worry about everything in the family, and she has already taken care of things I didn't think of. It makes people feel comfortable in spirit!)

(Second sister-in-law, what a pity!) Both Ruohua and Zhongnan stared at Youzhong, listening to him continue: (What a pity she is a woman! Otherwise, she would have the talent of a governor.)

Automobile News

Shanghai Automobile Statistics Exceed 15,000 Vehicles, Optimistic About the Future of the Automotive Business 203

Related to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway

The 1932 Shanghai car registration numbers have been announced, and the number has increased compared to previous years. Therefore, car dealers are not discouraged by the war last spring and the economic downturn. Although this increase cannot be compared with the years when business was booming, the total number of car registrations in the Public Concession and the French Concession reached 15,365 by December 31, 1932, excluding military vehicles. This is an increase of 544 vehicles compared to previous years. Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway on October 10, 1932, car dealers in Shanghai have been very satisfied with their 1933 business forecasts. The Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, including the national highway leading to Nanjing, has a total length of 350 miles for driving. According to the China Automobile Club, the second road paving project will be completed, and heavy vehicles will be able to pass through by May 1. There are also 400 miles of motorways near Hangzhou that are used daily. Although the completion of this road will not lead to a sudden increase in the number of cars in this city, many car dealerships along and near the highway have purchased used cars from Shanghai.

Recently, car users in Shanghai have improved their standards for cars compared to a year ago. As a result, there are fewer old and dilapidated cars on the market. Streamlined vehicles, which were once popular, are also plentiful here. Light vehicles have been quite popular recently because they are cheaper to buy and have lower monthly expenses. The amount of gasoline and lubricating oil they use is far less than that of larger cars. Vehicles manufactured by British factories are the most famous, but French, German, and Italian ones are also quite good.

In 1932, Ford still ranked first in Shanghai car registrations with 1,399 vehicles, including those manufactured by Ford's British factory. Morris surpassed Buick this time to take second place with 1,094 registrations. Buick had 1,008 vehicles. Chevrolet was in fourth place with 825 vehicles. Austin was fifth with 668 vehicles. Studebaker was slightly weaker with 562 vehicles. Fiat, a car manufactured in mainland China, ranked seventh with 541 registrations. The number of other brands of cars can be seen in the table below: Shanghai Automobile Statistics as of December 31, 1932

According to official statistics at the end of last year, there were a total of 3,289 freight vehicles in the city, compared to 3,370 on December 31, 1931, a decrease of 81 vehicles. When considering these figures, one point must be noted: a freight vehicle must be registered and taxed in two places when in use. Statistical disputes often arise due to overlapping. The number of freight vehicle registrations in the Public Concession decreased from 1,935 to 1,823, a decrease of 112 vehicles. The French Concession increased by 31 vehicles, with numbers of 1,435 compared to 1,466. This number may indicate an increase in freight vehicles in the French Concession, but it may not necessarily be a decrease in the Public Concession, as some car owners in the French Concession may not renew their Public Concession vehicle licenses. However, the freight vehicle business in the French Concession has indeed increased. The Ford and Studebaker brands have slightly declined compared to the past. The increase in Thornycroft Stevens vehicles indicates the development of the public transportation business.

Astonishing Performance of the New Standard Car 204

Two Thousand Miles of Travel in Nine Days

The latest Standard cars have been greatly improved in terms of manufacturing. Therefore, there are often astonishing results. Recently, a new 46-horsepower sedan was driven on rough roads, traveling 2,000 miles in nine days. The driver was Mr. Walding of the British Automobile and Motorcycle Association. According to reliable sources, this new car has already arrived in Shanghai and is on display in the showroom of the China Automobile Company. Its advantages are that it is fast and the parts are durable. The strength of the parts and the durability of the materials are essential advantages of Standard cars, and the new car must have even more improvements.

Another matter worth mentioning to the readers is that, in fact, from the moment the Standard car starts to the moment it reaches its destination, there are no obstacles whatsoever under any circumstances. When Mr. Walding tested the car, he drove it for nine days. Finally, he drove into Clingoe territory, in the Scottish region, which is perhaps the most dangerous place, and it is difficult for ordinary travelers to pass through there. However, in recent years, the authorities have built a highland road with a spirit of fearlessness, under difficult and arduous conditions. Only then have a few tourists traveled through it, but sometimes dangers still occur.

Between Augustus and Inverness, the driver had to drive south of Lochness. Glen Doe used to be a terrible mountain. When the driver reaches this mountain, he will inevitably feel terrified. Recalling several years ago, many light cars were driven on the mountain road. At that high place, they all had to be pushed by manpower. This time, the Standard car had no difficulties and drove safely. Even in dangerous places, it only used second gear. The soil along the way was loose and the air was fresh, which was especially suitable for the driver. The winding mountain roads, the crisscrossing rivers, the intermingling of water and clouds, and the villages standing side by side, all kinds of scenery cannot be described in words. In Inverness, a 2.6-ton six-cylinder Citroen truck, newly purchased by the French Water and Electricity Company from the French Da Automobile Company at 424 Avenue Joffre, is used to repair overhead wires.

In the journey of 2,000 miles, the roads passed were uneven. If the vehicle driving did not have considerable performance, it would not be able to reach its destination. There were many cars traveling together, and as a result of the journey, the performance of the new Standard car was the best, which is truly admirable. Moreover, when the car was running, not a single drop of water was added to the radiator. In other aspects of the parts, there were no defects that caused the car to stop. Even when driving at the highest speed on the worst roads, there was no excessive heat. Therefore, even in cold places, after stopping for a long time, there were no obstacles when starting. This kind of performance is not easy to see in ordinary cars.

The nine-day trip was quite interesting. On the first day, he traveled to Whafedel, which is halfway between Brough and Coldfell. Cars, motorcycles, and bicycles formed a line and drove through it, which was the most dangerous area. After Coldfell, the road surface was flatter and the danger was reduced. The driver was more at ease. After that, he passed through Kirkby, Tan Hill, and Alston, and from Saltaire to Melrose, he passed through Otterburn and Jedburgh and entered Scottish territory. Then the ground was flatter and a safe speed could be used.

When driving along the River Tweed and within Melrose, it suddenly rained that day. When driving in the rain, the beauty of the Standard car's body made the passengers sit comfortably in the car without feeling any discomfort. It was even more remarkable. In the evening, he arrived in Carlow. The rain was even heavier. All industries in the city were shut down. There was already a plan to stop moving forward. However, the Standard car, because of its perfect roof, could prevent wind and rain and drive safely. Two days later, he arrived in Inverness, passing through Aviemore and Grantown-on-Spey, and then reached Granton-on-Spey, which was also a rough road. However, the beauty of the scenery along the way was rare. Inverness, as a city in the Highlands, was regarded as the center point during the test drive. He drove for two days. Then, due to environmental reasons, he drove south and reached Ballater, which was a newly built road. (To be continued)
